# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FCrKHBJP6yFl8FeEvgJLq%2FGitbook%2520Offerwall.png&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9963699f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk#benefits)

Benefits


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk#features)

Features


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk#quick-links)

Quick links


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/samples)
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk#get-started)

Get Started


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk#supported-platforms)

Supported Platforms

[androidAndroid Integrationchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration)
[reactReact Nativechevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native)
[unityUnitychevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity)
[browserWebchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web)
[appleiOSchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk#reward-verification)

Reward Verification

[🦉Server-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configurationchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%2Fblobs%2FhKE0septTPS1i1HmgTdP%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=75e9a981&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5#benefits)

Benefits


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5#features)

Features


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.

# PubScale Onboarding | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#create-an-account)

Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.comarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#request-offerwall-sdk)

Request Offerwall SDK

The Offerwall SDK is currently released as an invite-only feature on the dashboard. You will have to request your account manager for this feature to be visible in your account after you have signed up on the dashboard.

Once you have the feature enabled, you can proceed with creating an app and the integration flow.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#creating-an-offerwall-unit)

Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once the feature is enabled, you can access it from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FJRKZiDS1kmUf31Npc1GX%252FGroup%252078578.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75aa1fef-914d-469c-88d1-9c343a79d13b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5ea54577&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252F1mnqbBerJIMUTJ4nGlQs%252FGroup%252078579.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2490a4e6-18f5-40dc-81bd-51bfbf7e79db&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f4c6e0d&sv=2)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FDYA7VLpYVh07yvNt7R49%252FGroup%252078580.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b1ba07c-c3df-40b7-8f5b-1f6b4950ae78&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f43f874&sv=2)

1.  Additionally, you can also setup S2S callbacks for better security.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252F9VYLKzFNkSK274ZbDUt4%252FGroup%252078580%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39d11794-8a12-4237-a22c-630e684604d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ecdb55af&sv=2)

[PreviousPrerequisiteschevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/prerequisites/prerequisites)
[NextSetting up the SDKchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)

# Setting up the SDK | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

Kotlin Script

Groovy

Copy

    dependencyResolutionManagement {
        repositoriesMode.set(RepositoriesMode.FAIL_ON_PROJECT_REPOS)
        repositories {
            maven { url = uri("https://storage.googleapis.com/caterpillar-libs-bucket/") }
        }
    }

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#id-4.-configure-proguard-rules)

4\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    
    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

# Initialize the SDK | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

Parameters for init call:

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

Kotlin

Java

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
       .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap) //optional
       .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foreground) //optional
       .setFullscreenEnabled(false) //optional
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
                   .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foregroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setFullscreenEnabled(false)//optional
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. Default: false

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

triangle-exclamation

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)

**Initialize the Offerwall SDK:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

Java

circle-info

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

circle-info

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

[PreviousSetting up the SDKchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWallchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/start-the-offerwall)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [Creating OfferWallConfig object:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)
    
*   [](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)
    
*   [Initialize the Offerwall SDK:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)
    

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, object : OfferWallInitListener {
       override fun onInitSuccess() {
       }
       override fun onInitFailed(error: InitError) {
       }
    })

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, new OfferWallInitListener() {
       @Override
       public void onInitSuccess() {
    
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onInitFailed(@NonNull InitError error) {
    
       }
    });

# Customization | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/customization#step-1-custom-loader-background-and-top-banner-background)

Press the preset button on your imported image and select the OfferWallTextureImporter preset from the menu and click apply.

Drag and drop the new image file inside the "Offer Wall Background Image" field located on OfferWall prefab.

# Adding the SDK | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/adding-the-sdk#id-1.-add-the-offerwall-unity-plugin-to-your-unity-project)

1\. Add the OfferWall Unity plugin to your Unity project

[Downloadarrow-up-right](https://github.com/GreedyGame/unity-offer_wall_plugin/releases/latest)
 and import the latest version of OfferWall Unity Plugin from GitHub.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/adding-the-sdk#id-2.-configuring-publishing-settings)

2\. Configuring Publishing Settings

Set the minimum API level to 24 or above and the target API level to 33 or above under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Other Settings

Check Custom Main Gradle template and Custom Gradle Properties Template under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Publishing Settings

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252F7fd3PoDMy8KiaYAWHDmu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db86f09f3-4e60-4de1-8259-ae6462fcdc57&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40910e43&sv=2)

Publishing settings

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/adding-the-sdk#id-3.-force-resolve-dependencies)

3\. Force resolve dependencies

**Force resolve** forces the Package Manager to resolve the project’s packages, reinstalling any altered or missing package and removing extraneous packages.

To Force resolve the dependencies, Goto Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve (if the resolver did not open automatically)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FUzYUObvgE35BpwNoljLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd15261f-4718-4073-ae62-8839fe558896&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4511d285&sv=2)

Drag and drop the OfferWallButton prefab from Assets > OfferWall > Prefabs > OfferWallButton.prefab under any canvas game object.

circle-exclamation

Please make sure you have the Android build grade version 4 and above.

# Initialize the SDK | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app API key (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

**user\_id:** Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#initializing-the-sdk)

Initializing the SDK

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "APP_ID", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

The SDK Initialization is complete. Learn how to launch the offerwall in the next step.

[PreviousSetting up the SDKchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWallchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/start-the-offerwall)

Last updated 2 years ago

---

# Pre integration checks | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

1\. Make sure you are using Unity version 2019.4.0f1 or above

2\. Android platform is selected for your Unity project.

3\. Use the App ID from the dashboard to initialize the SDK.

4\. Text Mesh Pro package installed in your Unity project.

5\. The Editor must support Android Gradle version 4.0.1 or above.

6\. Ensure your application builds without any errors before adding the plugin.

[PreviousStart the OfferWallchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/start-the-offerwall)
[NextAdding the SDKchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/adding-the-sdk)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Start the OfferWall | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

Java

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

circle-info

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

Java

[PreviousInitialize the SDKchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk)
[NextPre integration checkschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/pre-integration-checks)

Last updated 2 years ago

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallListener offerWallListener = new OfferWallListener() {
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onRewardClaimed(@NonNull Reward reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onFailed(@NonNull String message) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: " + message);
       }
    };

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener)            

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener);

# S2S Callback Configuration | 1.0.5 | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>
          
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward (in-app currency) earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

Golang

NodeJs

Python

PHP

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

circle-info

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

[PreviousStart the OfferWallchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/start-the-offerwall)
[NextSampleschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/samples)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [1\. Setup Callback URL](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)
    
*   [2\. Server Response](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)
    
*   [3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)
    

Copy

    
    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

Copy

    
    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    
    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            
        

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FNEZcqIt91K5sUcc4F4p5%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89fb849c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#benefits)

Benefits


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#features)

Features


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#quick-links)

Quick links


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/samples)
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#get-started)

Get Started


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

# FAQs | Offerwall SDK

chevron-rightHow do I create an PubScale Offerwall Placement/How do I get Offerwall App ID?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-do-i-create-an-pubscale-offerwall-placement-how-do-i-get-offerwall-app-id)

Refer to the content below.

[Setting up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)

chevron-rightHow do I show my currency icon on the PubScale Offerwall?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-do-i-show-my-currency-icon-on-the-pubscale-offerwall)

While setting up the offerwall, you can add an icon for your currency. This icon can also be uploaded later on the app details page after creating the offerwall.

chevron-rightHow do I test the Offerwall Integration?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-do-i-test-the-offerwall-integration)

To test the integration, you can make use of the [sandbox environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
. Sandbox environment will have test offers which are very easy to complete. Upon completion of these offers you will receive S2S postbacks on the configured Sandbox S2S URL.

chevron-rightHow to reach to the PubScale team?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-to-reach-to-the-pubscale-team)

Email us at [info@pubscale.comenvelope](mailto:info@pubscale.com)

chevron-rightHow to get approval for web integration?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-to-get-approval-for-web-integration)

Contact to your Account Manager or email us at [info@pubscale.comenvelope](mailto:info@pubscale.com)

# PubScale Onboarding | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#create-an-account)

Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.comarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#request-offerwall-sdk)

Request Offerwall SDK

The Offerwall SDK is currently released as an invite-only feature on the dashboard. You will have to request your account manager for this feature to be visible in your account after you have signed up on the dashboard.

Once you have the feature enabled, you can proceed with creating an app and the integration flow.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#creating-an-offerwall-unit)

Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once the feature is enabled, you can access it from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FAf87bVBcwfm91ayPxkmC%2FGroup%252078578.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7033533c&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FTm3NjNk68xHulfnhovVu%2FGroup%252078579.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=43ba75a1&sv=2)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2F3FmadD4fhapjKLcvwG1H%2FGroup%252078580.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89e39252&sv=2)

1.  Additionally, you can also setup S2S callbacks for better security.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FIT2oXIfOaXZlkY7QEWbz%2FGroup%252078580%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=276aaa09&sv=2)

[PreviousPrerequisiteschevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/prerequisites)
[NextSetting up the SDKchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)

# Flutter | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

**Note: Please use seperate app IDs for Android and iOS**

circle-info

You can view the example integration from [pub.devarrow-up-right](https://pub.dev/packages/pubscale_offerwall_plugin/example)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/flutter#id-1.-add-this-to-your-pubspec.yaml-file)

1\. Add this to your pubspec.yaml file


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your pubspec.yaml file

Copy

    dependencies:
        pubscale_offerwall_plugin: ^0.0.4

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/flutter#id-2.-rebuild-the-project)

2\. Rebuild the project


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/flutter#id-3.-initialize-the-offerwall)

3\. Initialize the Offerwall


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below code into the widget where you want to initialize the offerwall

Copy

    import 'package:pubscale_offerwall_plugin/pubscale_offerwall_plugin.dart';
    ..
    ..
    ..
    final _pubscaleOfferwallPlugin = PubscaleOfferwallPlugin();
    _pubscaleOfferwallPlugin.initializeOfferwall(
          'YOUR_APP_KEY', //PubScale app key
          'UNIQUE_ID', // Unique ID to identify your user
          false, //sandbox
          false, //fullscreen
        );

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/flutter#id-4.-launch-the-offerwall)

4\. Launch the Offerwall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below code into the widget where you want to launch the offerwall

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/flutter#id-5.-listen-to-offerwall-events)

5\. Listen to Offerwall events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can handle various states of the offerwall by listening to the events by adding the below code

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/flutter#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

6\. Setup S2S callbacks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/flutter#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

7\. Test the OfferWall


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, to test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

[PreviousReact Nativechevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native)
[NextUnitychevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity)

Last updated 6 months ago

    import 'package:pubscale_offerwall_plugin/pubscale_offerwall_plugin.dart';
    ..
    ..
    ..
    _pubscaleOfferwallPlugin.offerwallEvents.listen((event) {
            switch (event['event']) {
              case 'offerwall_init_success':
                print('offerwall_init_success');
                break;
              case 'offerwall_init_failed':
                print('offerwall_init_failed');
                break;
              case 'offerwall_showed':
                print('offerwall_showed');
                break;
              case 'offerwall_closed':
                print('offerwall_closed');
                break;
              case 'offerwall_reward':
                print('offerwall_reward: ${event['amount']} ${event['currency']}');
                break;
              case 'offerwall_launch_failed':
                print('offerwall_launch_failed. \nError: ${event['error']}')
                break;
            }
        });

# Promotions | Offerwall SDK

The **Promotions** feature empowers publishers to boost user engagement by offering bonus rewards for completing offers in your app. For example, if an offer typically rewards 100 coins, you can run a promotion to give users 120 coins (or any custom bonus) for a limited time.

Promotions are fully configurable in your PubScale Dashboard under the **Offerwall** section.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions#id-1.-creating-a-promotion)

1\. Creating a Promotion


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to the Offerwall section, open the Overview tab, select your app from the list, then click the Promotion card in your app’s dashboard to view or create promotions. Click **Create Promotion** to get started.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FkRDh67DyShELsB5sb70G%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-20%2520at%25202.59.31%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd202c1ed-5a10-4385-b899-edc2a6d0a85f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f66a3c10&sv=2)

circle-info

Only one promotion can be active at a time.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions#id-1.1.-promotion-details)

1.1. Promotion Details

Promotion Name

Internal name for your reference (not shown to users)

Promotion Display Name

Name shown to users on the offerwall (e.g., New Year Offer)

Increase Percentage

Enter the percentage by which you want to increase the default offer reward for users (e.g., 20 for +20% bonus, so a 100 coin reward becomes 120 coins).

Date Range

**Set when the promotion should be active** (Start/End date & time, local timezone is auto-applied).

**Note:** The promotion duration must be between 1 and 7 days (minimum 1 day, maximum 7 days).

Targeting

Optionally select target countries to include or exclude

Promotion Banner

(Optional) Upload a banner image to visually highlight your promotion (JPG/PNG, max 1MB)

circle-info

A live preview will appear in the right pane, instantly reflecting any changes you make.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FYQNqS9GBqNh2Vf8Hfwzl%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520at%252012.52.56%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf931623-84a3-4ae7-8ae2-285184ea0bec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a414ad6&sv=2)

circle-info

This promotional bonus is provided by you (the publisher) to drive user engagement. The cost of the extra reward will be deducted from your margin, not the advertiser’s.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions#id-2.-how-promotions-work)

2\. How Promotions Work

*   **User View:** Users see the promotion and the increased reward directly in the offerwall, along with your custom banner (if provided).
    
*   **Reward Calculation:** The user receives the base reward _plus_ the promotional bonus. _Example:_ If the base reward is 100 coins and the promotion is +20%, the user gets 120 coins.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions#id-3.-promotion-scheduling)

3\. Promotion Scheduling

*   **Start Immediately:** The promotion is active as soon as you create it.
    
*   **Start Later:** Set a custom start date and time.
    
*   **End Date:** The promotion automatically ends at your specified date and time.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252Fl1G2YeB3VXHVtMmFimLn%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520at%252010.13.30%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb1b6981-d021-4376-b266-7ecae029406e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9fe9fc4a&sv=2)

Promotions Actions (Edit/Enable/Disable)

💡 In the Offerwall > Promotions section, publishers can view all their promotions and easily edit, activate, deactivate any promotion directly from the list.

[PreviousServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configurationchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)
[NextSandbox Environmentchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Initialize the SDK | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app API key (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

**user\_id:** Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#initializing-the-sdk)

Initializing the SDK

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "APP_ID", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

The SDK Initialization is complete. Learn how to launch the offerwall in the next step.

[NextStart the OfferWallchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/start-the-offerwall)

# Setting up the SDK | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file

Kotlin Script

Groovy

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.7')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.7'

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-clean-build-and-rebuild-the-project)

2\. Clean build and Rebuild the project

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configure-proguard-rules)

3\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    -keep class com.pubscale.caterpillar.analytics.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-5.-add-native-module-files)

5\. Add native module files

Add the following files to your android app's module directory.

*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.javaarrow-up-right](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.java)
    
*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.javaarrow-up-right](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.java)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-6.-link-the-module)

6\. Link the module

Add the following line inside the getPackages() method of MainApplication class.

`packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage());`

# Start the OfferWall | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

Java

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

circle-info

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

Java

[PreviousInitialize the SDKchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk)
[NextSetting up the SDKchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)

Last updated 1 year ago

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallListener offerWallListener = new OfferWallListener() {
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onRewardClaimed(@NonNull Reward reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onFailed(@NonNull String message) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: " + message);
       }
    };

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener)

# Setting up the SDK | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk#id-1.-add-the-offerwall-unity-plugin-to-your-unity-project)

**1\. Add the OfferWall Unity plugin to your Unity project**

[Downloadarrow-up-right](https://github.com/GreedyGame/unity-offer_wall_plugin/releases/latest)
 and import the latest version of OfferWall Unity Plugin from GitHub.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-configuring-publishing-settings)

**2\. Configuring Publishing Settings**

*   Set the minimum API level to 24 or above and the target API level to 33 or above under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Other Settings
    
*   Make sure you check the below-mentioned checkboxes under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Publishing Settings.
    
    *   **Custom Main Manifest**
        
    *   **Custom Main Gradle Template**
        
    *   **Custom Gradle Settings Template**
        
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2425324002-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%252Fuploads%252FbhnbN0kpLWTXZNUiquh6%252FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25201.06.50%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f02e2a1-5b1b-414d-8e71-90035f1e1801&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=befc650d&sv=2)

Player > Publishing settings

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configuring-dependencies)

**3\. Configuring dependencies**

Adding `mavenCentral()` as a repository in `settingsTemplate.gradle`

Add the below line inside the dependencies block in your mainTemplate.gradle file

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk#id-4.-force-resolve-dependencies)

**4\. Force resolve dependencies**

**Force resolve** forces the Package Manager to resolve the project’s packages, reinstalling any altered or missing package and removing extraneous packages.

To Force resolve the dependencies, Goto Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve (if the resolver did not open automatically)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FUzYUObvgE35BpwNoljLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd15261f-4718-4073-ae62-8839fe558896&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c95a673969eca060eea708c9fdc31002608f810ed2f72bebef304fa7c837926b)

# Direct Link | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/web/direct-link#to-create-a-direct-link-to-pubscale-offerwall-add-an-anchor-tag-in-your-html-that-redirects-to-the-p)

To create a direct link to Pubscale Offerwall, add an anchor tag in your HTML that redirects to the Pubscale Offerwall. It's best to use an image or button rather than a text link for this purpose.

Copy

    <a href="https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}">
      <img src="path_to_your_image.png" alt="Pubscale Offerwall"> 
    </a>

Parameter

Required

Comment

app\_id

yes

Get it from the PubScale Dashboard

user\_id

yes

Unique User ID

# Launch the offerwall | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

Add the below code into the widget where you want to launch the offerwall from

Copy

    void launchOfferwall(String appId, String userId) async{
      await launchUrlInCustomTabs(
        Uri.parse("https://wow.pubscale.com/?app_id=${appId}&user_id=${userId}"),
      );
    }
    
    Future<void> launchUrlInCustomTabs(Uri uri) async {
      final theme = Theme.of(context);
      try {
        await launchUrl(
          uri,
          options: LaunchOptions(
            barColor: theme.colorScheme.surface,
            onBarColor: theme.colorScheme.onSurface,
            barFixingEnabled: false,
          ),
        );
      } catch (e) {
          // If the URL launch fails, an exception will be thrown. (For example, if no browser app is installed on the Android device.)
        debugPrint(e.toString());
      }
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/flutter/launch-the-offerwall#launching-the-offerwall)

Launching the Offerwall

To launch the offerwall, simply call the launchOfferwall() method with the pubscale app id and your app's user id as the parameters.

[NextPreintegration Checkschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/preintegration-checks)

Last updated 1 year ago

    launchOfferwall("OFFERWALL_APP_ID", "USER_ID");

# iOS | Offerwall SDK

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#id-1.-integration)

1\. Integration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FqezM0kmxXdVWJkgQBBok%2FWow_flow%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a4dde4a&sv=2)![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FluDiQcm4sdLejDTuGlzU%2Fwow_flow_dark.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef70fe3f&sv=2)

To integrate the PubScale Offerwall, you need to construct a URL and provide a set of parameters for proper configuration.

**Construct the Offerwall URL**

**Parameters**

Parameters

Description

**app\_id** (Required)

This is the unique identifier for your app, required for integration.

**user\_id** (Required)

A unique identifier for each user, required to track their activity on the offerwall. We recommend using a UUID as the user\_id.

**idfa** (Optional but Recommended)

For iOS integrations Include the **idfa** as a parameter when launching the Offerwall. This helps enhance tracking accuracy and plays a key role in fraud prevention.

To integrate the PubScale Offerwall into your iOS App, you have the following options:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#using-sfsafariviewcontroller)

Using SFSafariViewController:

For optimal performance and user experience, we recommend launching the Offerwall using `SFSafariViewController`

Here's a simple Swift example that opens PubScale Offerwall in a `SFSafariViewController` on iOS

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#notes)

Notes:

*   This code should be placed in a `UIViewController` subclass.
    
*   You can call `openLinkInSafariViewController()` when appropriate (e.g., on a button tap or in `viewDidLoad` as shown).
    
*   Don't forget to import `SafariServices`.
    
*   Don't forget to replace the {app\_id} ,{user\_id} and {idfa} with the actula value.
    
*   If your App is not approved from PubScale you might see an error page. ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FHacO5ha0ife9UqM2nrQL%2FScreenshot%25202025-04-23%2520at%25205.19.10%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39932216&sv=2) If you see this error,
    
    *   Check your App ID and make sure it is correct.
        
    *   If your App ID is correct then its possible your App ID is not approved yet, in that case please reach out to your Account Manager to get your App approved.
        
    
    If your configuration is correct, you will see a page similar to the screenshot below. ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FP7eukHoE3cc0C4YrsoCC%2FScreenshot%25202025-04-23%2520at%25205.30.08%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bce9ed7b&sv=2)
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

3\. Test the OfferWall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

To ensure your OfferWall integration is working perfectly, follow these steps during the testing phase.

*   Open the offerwall and verify that all offers are displayed correctly.
    
*   Complete an offer and confirm that a callback is received from PubScale server to your server. For the sandbox environment, ensure the callback URL is configured properly to receive sandbox callbacks.
    
*   Ensure the hashing technique used matches the one specified in the documentation.
    
*   Verify that the reward value received matches the value displayed for the offer.
    
*   Confirm that the callback is received only from PubScale's [whitelisted server IPs](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)
    .
    

[PreviousWebchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web)
[NextAPIchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api)

*   [1\. Integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#id-1.-integration)
    
*   [Using SFSafariViewController:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#using-sfsafariviewcontroller)
    
*   [2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)
    
*   [3\. Test the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}&idfa={idfa}

Copy

    import UIKit
    import SafariServices
    
    class ViewController: UIViewController {
    
        override func viewDidLoad() {
            super.viewDidLoad()
            openLinkInSafariViewController()
        }
    
        func openLinkInSafariViewController() {
            if let url = URL(string: "https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}&idfa={idfa}") {
                let safariVC = SFSafariViewController(url: url)
                safariVC.modalPresentationStyle = .formSheet
                present(safariVC, animated: true, completion: nil)
            } else {
                print("Invalid URL")
            }
        }
    }

[Setting up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)

chevron-rightHow do I show my currency icon on the PubScale Offerwall?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/faqs#how-do-i-show-my-currency-icon-on-the-pubscale-offerwall)

While setting up the offerwall, you can add an icon for your currency. This icon can also be uploaded later on the app details page after creating the offerwall.

chevron-rightHow do I test the Offerwall Integration?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/faqs#how-do-i-test-the-offerwall-integration)

To test the integration, you can make use of the [sandbox environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
. Sandbox environment will have test offers which are very easy to complete. Upon completion of these offers you will receive S2S postbacks on the configured Sandbox S2S URL.

Adding PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage to React packages

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native#id-4.-initialize-the-sdk)

4\. Initialize the SDK


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app\_id (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

circle-info

Obtain your **app\_id** from the [PubScale Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
 by [adding your app and configuring the offerwall.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
 Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

Parameter

Description

**user\_id**

Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64**

An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64**

An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

**sandbox**

Enables the sandbox environment for the Offerwall Session

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native#id-4.1.-making-the-init-call)

4.1. Making the Init call

circle-info

Use sandbox parameter for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native#id-5.-start-the-offerwall)

5\. Start the OfferWall


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start the offerwall, just call, `PubscaleOfferwall.launch()` method.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

6\. Setup S2S callbacks


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

7\. Test the OfferWall


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

Copy

    packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallPackage())

Copy

    packages.add(PubscaleOfferwallPackage())

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //Initializes the SDK
    //call init once the user is logged in
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "app_id", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "sandbox": false, //set it to true to enable sandbox mode
        "background_Base64": base64Image, //optional
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callback
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

Copy

    PubscaleOfferwall.launch(
      () => {
        // Offerwall Showed Callback
        console.log("Offerwall launched");
      },
      () => {
        // Offerwall Closed Callback
        console.log("Offerwall closed");
      },
      (amt, curr, token) => {
        // Offerwall Rewarded Callback
        console.log("Reward:", amt, curr, token);
      },
      (err) => {
        // Offerwall Error Callback
        console.log("Launch error:", err);
      }
    );

# Setting up your app | Offerwall SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-1.-create-an-account)

1\. Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.comarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-2.-creating-an-offerwall-unit)

2\. Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once you have signed in, you can access Offerwall from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FIUK75Defcij42uSdSQN1%2FGroup%252078578.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c33f374&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FvIbmAuD4uMH5SBx0LxED%2FGroup%252078579.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=638569f1&sv=2)

1.  Once you’ve created your app in the dashboard and selected the desired integration type (Android SDK, Web Integration, or API), your app will enter a **Pending Approval** state.
    

circle-exclamation

The approval process is **asynchronous** and typically takes **up to 72 hours** as our team manually reviews each submission.

This **does not block your integration** process. We strongly recommend proceeding with the integration immediately. You can use **sandbox mode** to view and test offers while your app is pending approval.

Please make sure to follow the **integration checklist** to ensure you don’t miss any required steps before going live. Once the app is approved, it may take up to 5 minutes for all changes to fully propagate. If you encounter any errors, please wait for 5 minutes after receiving the approval confirmation.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-3.-before-you-go-live)

3\. Before you go live

You can find the checklist by clicking on the **Integration Steps** card

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FcKbcguIEQbGYUHREglfd%2FScreenshot%25202025-05-21%2520at%252012.55.22%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e3fc037&sv=2)

Please make sure you have completed all the steps in the checklist and mark it as completed.

# Android Integration | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

circle-info

You can download the Sample integration from [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/greedygame/demo-offerwall-android)

Integration video

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file. Once added, clean build and rebuild the project.

Kotlin Script

Groovy

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-2.-configure-proguard-rules)

2\. Configure proguard rules


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-initializing-the-offerwall)

3\. Initializing the OfferWall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.1.-parameters-for-init-call)

**3.1. Parameters for init call:**

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.2.-creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**3.2. Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

circle-info

Obtain your **PubScale app ID** from the [PubScale Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
 by [adding your app and configuring the offerwall.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
 Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

Java

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setSandboxEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in the sandbox environment

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. This can be used in apps or games where an immersive experience is needed. Default: false

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

triangle-exclamation

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.3.-making-the-init-call)

**3.3. Making the init call:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

Java

circle-exclamation

Make sure to handle Offerwall init failures properly as the init might fail in scenarios where the PubScale system detects a fraudulent environment.

circle-info

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-4.-start-the-offerwall)

4\. Start the OfferWall


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

Java

circle-info

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

Java

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

5\. Setup S2S callbacks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

6\. Test the OfferWall


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

[NextReact Nativechevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native)

# Initialize the SDK | 1.0.6-beta1 | Offerwall SDK

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app API key (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

**user\_id:** Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#initializing-the-sdk)

Initializing the SDK

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "APP_ID", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

The SDK Initialization is complete. Learn how to launch the offerwall in the next step.

[NextStart the OfferWallchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/start-the-offerwall)

# Preintegration Checks | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

1.  Make sure you are using Unity version 2019.4.0f1 or above
    
2.  Ensure your application builds without any errors before adding the plugin.
    
3.  Android platform is selected for your Unity project.
    
4.  The Editor must support Android Gradle version 4.0.1 or above.
    

[PreviousLaunch the offerwallchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/flutter/launch-the-offerwall)
[NextSetting up the SDKchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk)
