# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | 1.0.9 | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1235736282-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%252Fuploads%252FIQmczo2TwxZ41xb2d8KF%252FGitbook%2520Offerwall.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbd06600-574c-40dd-817f-115a71ff68b2&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c85820c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#benefits)

Benefits


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#features)

Features


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#quick-links)

Quick links


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/samples)
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#get-started)

Get Started


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

# Initialize the SDK | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

Parameters for init call:

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

Java

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
       .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap) //optional
       .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foreground) //optional
       .setFullscreenEnabled(false) //optional
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
                   .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foregroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setFullscreenEnabled(false)//optional
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. Default: false

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

triangle-exclamation

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)

**Initialize the Offerwall SDK:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

Java

circle-info

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

circle-info

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

# Start the OfferWall | 1.0.6-beta1 | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

Java

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

circle-info

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

Java

    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener);

---

# Unity | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#preintegration-checks)

[✅ arrow-up-right](https://www.alt-codes.net/check-mark-symbols.php)
Preintegration checks


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Make sure you are using Unity version 2019.4.0f1 or above
    
*   Ensure your application builds without any errors before adding the plugin.
    
*   Android platform is selected for your Unity project.
    
*   The Editor must support Android Gradle version 4.0.1 or above.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-1.-add-the-offerwall-unity-plugin-to-your-unity-project)

**1\. Add the OfferWall Unity plugin to your Unity project**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Downloadarrow-up-right](https://github.com/GreedyGame/unity-offer_wall_plugin/releases/latest)
 and import the latest version of OfferWall Unity Plugin from GitHub.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-publishing-settings)

**2\. Configuring Publishing Settings**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Set the minimum API level to 24 or above and the target API level to 33 or above under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Other Settings
    
*   Make sure you check the below-mentioned checkboxes under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Publishing Settings.
    
    *   **Custom Main Manifest**
        
    *   **Custom Main Gradle Template**
        
    *   **Custom Gradle Settings Template**
        
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2Fc6755ygeGSEINb02qqBB%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25201.06.50%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ec78d25&sv=2)

Player > Publishing settings

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-configuring-dependencies)

**3\. Configuring dependencies**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Adding `mavenCentral()` as a repository in `settingsTemplate.gradle`

Add the below line inside the dependencies block in your mainTemplate.gradle file

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-4.-force-resolve-dependencies)

**4\. Force resolve dependencies**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Force resolve** forces the Package Manager to resolve the project’s packages, reinstalling any altered or missing package and removing extraneous packages.

To Force resolve the dependencies, Goto Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve (if the resolver did not open automatically)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FUzYUObvgE35BpwNoljLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd15261f-4718-4073-ae62-8839fe558896&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c95a673969eca060eea708c9fdc31002608f810ed2f72bebef304fa7c837926b)

Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve

circle-info

OfferWall does not work in the Editor. Please use a real device to test the integration.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-1.-configuring-prefabs)

5\. Configuring Prefabs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#drag-and-drop-pubscaleofferwallobject-prefab)

**Drag and Drop** PubScaleOfferwallObject **prefab**

Drag and drop the **PubScaleOfferwallObject prefab** from Assets/OfferWall/Prefab/PubScaleOfferwallObject.prefab in the scene.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key)

6\. Configuring App Key


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter your PubScale app ID inside the "Pubscale App ID" field located on the PubScaleOfferwallObject.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FwXKwHwjjxnFJ1aVU0btm%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25202.05.03%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=119303b2&sv=2)

Offerwall Prefab

circle-info

The PubScale App ID is an 8-digit identifier generated during the app creation process within the dashboard. If you need help creating an account/app with us, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-1)

7\. Initialize the SDK


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To launch the OfferWall, call the PubScaleOfferwallClient.Initialize(string userId) function using the instance from PubScaleOfferwallObject prefab.

circle-info

Expected params:

1.  userID: A string value that is used to identify the user uniquely in your application. If this value is null, the SDK would internally create a userId for the device.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-2)

8\. Custom loader background image and foreground image


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FIjOqaG6yfsVp2ELfDOuX%2FGroup%252078600.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94c5d9a3&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#step-1-custom-loader-background-and-loader-foreground)

**Step 1: Custom loader background and loader foreground**

To use custom background and foreground images for the loading screen replace the **demo\_background\_img and demo\_foreground\_img** file located under Assets/OfferWall/Resources with the image you need.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#step-2-enable-read-and-write-under-advance-image-settings)

**Step 2: Enable Read and Write under Advance Image settings**

Press the preset button on your imported image and then select the OfferWallTextureImporter preset from the menu and click apply.

circle-info

If the fields are left empty, the default values will be used:

*   Background: Black image
    
*   Foreground: App icon
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-3)

9\. Set Offerwall Orientation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, the Offerwall opens in Portrait orientation. If you want to change this behaviour, do the following changes.

Add the below line inside the <application></application> tag in your AndroidManifest.xml file.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-4)

10\. Handling the SDK callbacks (optional)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To handle the SDK callbacks, subscribe to the events that are made available by the SimpleIntegration script.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-5)

11\. Launch the OfferWall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To launch the OfferWall, call the AdvancedIntegration.ShowOfferWall() function using the PubScaleOfferwallAdvanced prefab.

Can also be used in onClick of a button:

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2F66dd1yeG5dgShyYthB12%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25202.09.42%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed9a457&sv=2)

Example usage: Launching Offerwall on click of a button

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

11\. Setup S2S callbacks


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

12\. Test the OfferWall


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

Copy

    //Define functions that would be called when the callbacks are given
    void OnSDKInitSuccess() {
        
    }
    
    void OnSDKInitFailed(string message) {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallShowed() {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallClosed() {
        
    }
    
    void OnRewardClaimed(Reward reward) {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallFailed(string message) {
        
    }
    
    //Subscribe to the events
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnSDKInitSuccess += OnSDKInitSuccess;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnSDKInitFailed += OnSDKInitFailed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallShowed += OnOfferwallShowed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallClosed += OnOfferwallClosed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnRewardClaimed += OnRewardClaimed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallFailed += OnOfferwallFailed;

# Start the OfferWall | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `PubscaleOfferwall.launch()` method.

Copy

    PubscaleOfferwall.launch(() => {
        console.log("close"); //onClose
    }, (errMsg) => {
        console.log(errMsg); //onFailure
    });

chevron-rightHow do I create an PubScale Offerwall Placement/How do I get Offerwall App ID?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/faqs#how-do-i-create-an-pubscale-offerwall-placement-how-do-i-get-offerwall-app-id)

chevron-rightHow do I show my currency icon on the PubScale Offerwall?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/faqs#how-do-i-show-my-currency-icon-on-the-pubscale-offerwall)

While setting up the offerwall, you can add an icon for your currency. This icon can also be uploaded later on the app details page after creating the offerwall.

chevron-rightHow do I test the Offerwall Integration?[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/faqs#how-do-i-test-the-offerwall-integration)

To test the integration, you can make use of the [sandbox environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
. Sandbox environment will have test offers which are very easy to complete. Upon completion of these offers you will receive S2S postbacks on the configured Sandbox S2S URL.

Contact to your Account Manager or email us at [info@pubscale.comenvelope](mailto:info@pubscale.com)

# Web | Offerwall SDK

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-1.-integration)

1\. Integration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FqezM0kmxXdVWJkgQBBok%2FWow_flow%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a4dde4a&sv=2)![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%2Fblobs%2FluDiQcm4sdLejDTuGlzU%2Fwow_flow_dark.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef70fe3f&sv=2)

To integrate the PubScale Offerwall, you need to provide a set of mandatory parameters for proper configuration.

**Parameters**

Parameters

Description

**app\_id** (Required)

This is the unique identifier for your app, required for integration.

**user\_id** (Required)

A unique identifier for each user, required to track their activity on the offerwall. We recommend using a UUID as the user\_id.

**idfa** (Optional)

For iOS integrations Include the **idfa** as a parameter when launching the Web Offerwall. This helps enhance tracking accuracy and plays a key role in fraud prevention.

**ga\_id** (Optional)

For Android integrations Include the **ga\_id** as a parameter when launching the Web Offerwall. This helps enhance tracking accuracy and plays a key role in fraud prevention.

To integrate the PubScale Web Offerwall into your website, you have the following options:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-1.1.-using-an-iframe)

**1.1. Using an iframe**:

Place the following iframe in your HTML:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-1.2.-using-a-direct-link)

**1.2. Using a Direct Link**:

Create a direct link to the PubScale Offerwall using an anchor tag. It is recommended to use an image or button for better user experience:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-1.3.-using-javascript)

**1.3. Using JavaScript:**

Open the offerwall link programmatically using `window.open`. This provides flexibility for custom implementations.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

3\. Test the OfferWall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

To ensure your OfferWall integration is working perfectly, follow these steps during the testing phase.

*   Open the web offerwall and verify that all offers are displayed correctly.
    
*   Complete an offer and confirm that a callback is received from PubScale server to your server. For the sandbox environment, ensure the callback URL is configured properly to receive sandbox callbacks.
    
*   Ensure the hashing technique used matches the one specified in the documentation.
    
*   Verify that the reward value received matches the value displayed for the offer.
    
*   Confirm that the callback is received only from PubScale's [whitelisted server IPs](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)
    .
    

circle-exclamation

While you can use the Web Offerwall in an Android app through a WebView or Custom Chrome Tabs, we have observed better performance and fewer chargebacks when using PubScale's dedicated SDKs. PubScale provides dedicated SDKs for [Android](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration)
, [React Native](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/react-native)
, and [Unity](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity)
, which offer more secure and efficient integration methods. Please consider using these SDKs for better integration.

[PreviousUnitychevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/unity)
[NextiOSchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios)

*   [1\. Integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-1.-integration)
    
*   [1.1. Using an iframe:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-1.1.-using-an-iframe)
    
*   [1.2. Using a Direct Link:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-1.2.-using-a-direct-link)
    
*   [1.3. Using JavaScript:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-1.3.-using-javascript)
    
*   [2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)
    
*   [3\. Test the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/web#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

    <iframe id="pubscale-wow-iframe" src="https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}"></iframe>

Copy

    <a href="https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}">
      <img src="path_to_your_image.png" alt="PubScale Offerwall">
    </a>

Copy

    const appId = "your_app_id"; // Replace with your app ID
    const userId = "your_user_id"; // Replace with your unique user ID
    const offerwallUrl = `https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id=${appId}&user_id=${userId}`;
    
    window.open(offerwallUrl, '_blank');

# Initialize the SDK | 1.0.6-beta1 | Offerwall SDK

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

Parameters for init call:

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

Java

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
       .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap) //optional
       .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foreground) //optional
       .setFullscreenEnabled(false) //optional
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
                   .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foregroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setFullscreenEnabled(false)//optional
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. Default: false

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

triangle-exclamation

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)

**Initialize the Offerwall SDK:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

Java

circle-info

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

circle-info

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

# S2S Callback Configuration | 1.0.7 | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>
          
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

Golang

NodeJs

Python

PHP

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

circle-info

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

[PreviousDirect Linkchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/web/direct-link)
[NextIP Whitelistchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [1\. Setup Callback URL](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)
    
*   [2\. Server Response](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)
    
*   [3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)
    

Copy

    
    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

Copy

    
    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    
    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            
        

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

.

circle-info

1.  userID: A string value that is used to identify the user uniquely in your application. If this value is null, the SDK would internally create a userId for the device.

# Start the OfferWall | 1.0.6-beta1 | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `PubscaleOfferwall.launch()` method.

Copy

    PubscaleOfferwall.launch(() => {
        console.log("close"); //onClose
    }, (errMsg) => {
        console.log(errMsg); //onFailure
    });

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2F1FwlfQTU4NySYZsBbL5m%2FGitbook%2520Offerwall.png&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e74458ff&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10#benefits)

Benefits


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10#features)

Features


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10#quick-links)

Quick links


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/samples)
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10#get-started)

Get Started


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10#supported-platforms)

# Sandbox Environment | Offerwall SDK

The Sandbox environment allows you to fully test the integration before releasing your app to production. You can simulate the complete workflow from SDK initialization to receiving callbacks without affecting the live environment.

circle-info

Your app does not need to be live or published to use the Sandbox environment.

* * *

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#launch-sandbox)

Launch SandBox


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FwrZvgCeUlDm78zCmrR8m%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-16%2520at%25206.10.05%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4aa3c5fd-20f9-414f-977e-0efe3e7e074e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63f845a1&sv=2)

Launch Sandbox mode

**Launch the Sandbox**: Click **Launch Sandbox** to begin testing your integration.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252F3Zeao4OQxzQ66GukIlNL%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-16%2520at%25206.19.39%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dccb42901-ea57-4fce-9a86-062e433fa173&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25638c12&sv=2)

Enter an User ID for getting logs

Input a test User ID and click **Go**.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#setting-user-id-during-sdk-initialization)

Setting User ID During SDK Initialization

Android

Web

API

Call `setUniqueId("YOUR_USER_ID")` during SDK initialization.

Set Unique user id by passing a query param`?user_id=YOUR_USER_ID`

In the tracking link provided, Append Unique user id as query param `user_id: YOUR_USER_ID`

> **Important:** The User ID you enter here must be the same as the User ID used in your SDK initialization. This ensures that all events and callbacks are properly linked and you receive the test callback for this user.

* * *

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#enable-sandbox-mode)

Enable Sandbox Mode


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Android

Web

API

Call `setSandboxEnabled(true)` during SDK initialization.

Enable sandbox mode by passing a query param`?sandbox=true`

Get sandbox mode offers by passing the sandbox key in the API body as `sandbox: true`

* * *

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#system-logs)

System Logs


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FmDBgLVhTO05bWBn3o6Ah%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-17%2520at%25202.59.04%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6d34c3e-9563-41a4-8e5d-2ee6e6b2a56e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcbeeccb&sv=2)

System logs

**Trigger Events**: Perform actions in your application. Corresponding events will be logged in the **System Logs**.

circle-info

Resetting the history will clear all offer progress for this user, allowing you to retest offers from the start.

💡 You can configure a **Server-to-Server (S2S) callback** to receive event data directly on your server. Check [Integeration Steps](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)
.

circle-info

If you are able to see all expected events in the System Logs and receive callbacks correctly during your Sandbox testing, you can be confident that your integration is set up properly and ready for production.

[NextSampleschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/samples)

Kotlin Script

Groovy

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta1')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta1'

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-clean-build-and-rebuild-the-project)

2\. Clean build and Rebuild the project

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configure-proguard-rules)

3\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    
    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

# Server-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration | Offerwall SDK

Server-to-Server callbacks allow you to receive reward confirmation events directly from the offerwall via HTTP requests.

Go to the Offerwall section, open the Overview tab, select your app from the list, then click the S2S Callbacks card in your app’s dashboard to create or manage S2S callbacks. Click **Configure** to get started.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FzEQj296qHxykXUbkYIqp%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-20%2520at%25205.09.44%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8a9856a-fc29-45e5-8b64-6f272aca7670&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d136f68c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a user completes an offer and earns a reward, an HTTP GET request is sent to your configured callback URL. The request includes a set of query parameters that convey key reward information.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.1.-base-url)

1.1. Base URL

You must first define your **Base URL** — the endpoint on your server that will handle the incoming callback.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252F8iNeskzGNy3z3U7hyZdv%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520at%25203.25.01%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2682d4c5-21f1-4841-a368-653f73092afe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b9bb805&sv=2)

BaseUrl and Final Callback Url

circle-info

For any custom URL requirements or special customizations, please contact your Account Manager.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.2.-parameter-configuration)

1.2. Parameter Configuration

Parameters can be added using a **key-value builder** interface:

*   Keys are fully editable.
    
*   Values are selected from predefined **macros** (e.g., `user_id`, `value`, etc.) via a searchable dropdown.
    
*   **Static parameters** can also be added with hardcoded values.
    
*   Some **default system parameters** are pre-filled (e.g., `user_id`, `value`, `token`, `signature`) and appear in the list with locked values.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FrJd4TIhliisUZjbJxsgI%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520at%252012.49.16%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f2b044e-3ad1-4461-984d-e9d17b2539cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3111d4e&sv=2)

Callback Macros Key Values

circle-info

**Example callback setup:**

**Callback URL set by you:** http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale

**Request sent from us:** HTTP GET http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user\_id={user\_id}&value={value}&token={token}&signature={signature}

Query Params

Description

user\_id \*

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value \*

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token \*

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature \*

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

click\_datetime

The Unix timestamp of when the user clicked the offer. Eg`1718509200`

conversion\_datetime

The Unix timestamp of when the user completed the offer. Eg `1718509400`

country

The user's country in ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 code. Example: `IN`, `US`

gaid

The user's Google Advertising ID (Android only). Example: `a1b2c3d4-e5f6-7890-gh12-ijkl3456mnop`

goal\_name

The name assigned to the reward or task. Example: `Complete 5th Level`

goal\_value

A unique code for the completed task. Example: `FB_Level_Complete_5`

idfa

Apple’s Identifier for Advertisers (iOS only). Example: `6D92078A-8246-4BA4-AE5B-76104861E7DC`

ip

The IP address of the user when the offer was clicked. Example: `192.168.0.101`

offer\_id

A unique identifier for the completed offer. Example: `45678`

offer\_name

The title of the completed offer. Example: `Tappy Plane - GameApp`

package\_name

The package name of the app associated with the offer. Example: `com.tappyplane.gameapp`

payout\_usd

The payout amount in USD for the completed offer. Example: `0.75`

useragent

The user’s browser and device information string. Example: `Mozilla/5.0 (Linux; Android 10; Pixel 3)`

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.3.-server-response)

1.3. Server Response


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.4.-hash-validation)

1.4. Hash validation

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

PHP

NodeJs

Python

Golang

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FxQrlXbH5BpGuJKbCLNP0%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520at%252012.46.13%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09b360d2-df50-4939-8187-b72ad495bddf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94deafe8&sv=2)

circle-info

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.5.-ip-whitelisting)

1.5. IP Whitelisting

You can restrict the callbacks to be accepted only from our sever IP address(es). Please whitelist the following IP(s) and regularly check back to find possible changes

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-test-callback-tool)

2\. Test Callback Tool


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A dedicated modal tool is available to test your callback configuration before going live.

*   Safely edit and test the callback URL without impacting your saved configuration.
    
*   **Input Fields**:
    
    *   **User ID**: Used to simulate a user session.
        
    *   **Custom Reward Value**: Used to simulate a reward payout.
        
    
*   This allows for quick verification of your endpoint and debugging of parameters.
    

circle-info

The User ID you enter here must be the same as the User ID used in your SDK initialization

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FWpLrYFKQpexjeZJIU65Z%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520at%25208.09.15%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15516315-d190-4365-8a2d-9744a3c57aaa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4322436&sv=2)

[PreviousAPIchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api)
[NextPromotionschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [1\. Setup Callback URL](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)
    
*   [1.1. Base URL](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.1.-base-url)

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

Copy

    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            

Copy

    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }

# Server-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration | 1.0.9 | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

circle-info

**Example callback setup:**

**Callback URL set by you:** http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale

**Request sent from us:** HTTP GET http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user\_id=<user\_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>      
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

# Setting up the SDK | 1.0.6-beta1 | Offerwall SDK

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file

Kotlin Script

Groovy

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta1')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta1'

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-clean-build-and-rebuild-the-project)

2\. Clean build and Rebuild the project

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configure-proguard-rules)

3\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-5.-add-native-module-files)

5\. Add native module files

Add the following files to your android app's module directory.

*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.javaarrow-up-right](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.java)
    
*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.java](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-6.-link-the-module)

6\. Link the module

Add the following line inside the getPackages() method of MainApplication class.

`packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage());`

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcJjYVtSXK83YJkG3H9nv%2Fblobs%2Foos3IZWjwdVDEtjRGJF7%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd15d9&sv=2)

Adding PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage to React packages

We have setup the SDK in the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | 1.0.6-beta2 | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F47uqFPZw7HlLBl2j2OyM%2Fblobs%2FISBQsuHhQwZxtdY4gfTy%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=adb43078&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#benefits)

Benefits


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#features)

Features


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#quick-links)

Quick links


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/samples)
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#get-started)

Get Started


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

[📪Prerequisiteschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/prerequisites)
[Native Androidchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)
[React Nativechevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[🦉S2S Callback Configurationchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration)

[NextPrerequisiteschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/prerequisites)

# Setting up your app | 1.0.9 | Offerwall SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-1.-create-an-account)

1\. Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.comarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-2.-creating-an-offerwall-unit)

2\. Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once you have signed in, you can access Offerwall from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FK5zkwq5a6L9tULQEuu2S%2FGroup%252078578.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=269e7d66&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FEg7kFlIY1r6SxaZZf4cd%2FGroup%252078579.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a339a59b&sv=2)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2F4sia7rIl4kIp4hANnnk8%2FGroup%252078580.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a5450486&sv=2)

1.  You can setup S2S callbacks here for better security and instant updates on rewards.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2F5BaUpl4HJpReLhU4i3Ka%2FGroup%252078580%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6dcd9d5d&sv=2)

[PreviousWelcome to PubScale Offerwall SDKchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9)
[NextAndroid Integrationchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration)

# PubScale Onboarding | 1.0.6-beta2 | Offerwall SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#create-an-account)

Create an account

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#request-offerwall-sdk)

Request Offerwall SDK

The Offerwall SDK is currently released as an invite-only feature on the dashboard. You will have to request your account manager for this feature to be visible in your account after you have signed up on the dashboard.

Once you have the feature enabled, you can proceed with creating an app and the integration flow.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#creating-an-offerwall-unit)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.

# API | Offerwall SDK

By integrating this API, publishers can seamlessly fetch and display these offers within their own user interface. This allows for the creation of fully native and personalised in-app experiences that align with the app’s design and user flow, enhancing user engagement and improving conversion rates.

triangle-exclamation

Pre-approval from PubScale team is required for the offerwall integration. Please contact your account manager or reach out to support before starting this integration. [Learn More](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-to-approval-for-web-integration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#id-1.-authentication)

1\. Authentication


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to access offers API. Following Keys need to be generated.

1.  Pub Key (Generated once per publisher)
    
2.  App ID
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#app-id)

App-ID

In order to generate an App ID follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit App ID. This will be used as App ID to access the API.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#pub-key)

Pub-Key

In order the generate a Pub-Key a pre-approval is required. This is a one time approval for a publisher. Please contact account manager for the same.

Go to the **Settings > API Key** section to get your Offerwall Pub-Key.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FpHekR6tktfVv57Crf3nB%252Fimage%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D203634b7-de9b-422d-8c70-0bf44830a8d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15e35d0e&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

You can regenerate the Pub-Key by contacting your Account Manager. Once the Offerwall Pub-Key is regenerated, the existing Pub-Key will no longer be valid.

* * *

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#id-2.-offers-api)

2\. Offers API:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#description)

Description:

The API provides a list of offers available for your app, which can be used to display and run offers on your platform.

circle-exclamation

Offers are cached on our server and refreshed every 5 minutes. We recommend updating your inventory accordingly.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#endpoint)

Endpoint:

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#auth)

Auth:

The keys generated in the previous steps must be included in the following headers when making API requests.

These are **Mandatory** for accessing the API.

*   **App-Id** – The unique App ID generated for your app during the setup process.
    
*   **Pub-Key** – The unique key generated for your publisher account during setup. This key is shared across all apps within the same account.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#example)

Example:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#payload)

Payload:

Body

Required

Type

Description

page

Required

Integer

The `page` field in the Offers API response indicates the current page number and should always be a positive integer.

size

Required

Integer

The `size` field in the Offers API response represents the number of offers returned in that response and should always be a positive integer.

filt

Optional

Array

Contains an array of filters to be applied to the Offers API request to refine the results based on specified criteria.

dim

Optional

String

Specifies the dimension on which the filter is applied. Supported values are `offer_type`, `platform`, and `country`.

match

Optional

Model

Contains details about the filter to be applied, including the values to filter by and the match type used for filtering.

type

Optional

String

Specifies the match type to be used for the filter. Supported values are `any` (matches any of the provided values) and `exact` (requires a single, exact value match).

values

Optional

Array

Contains the values to apply the filter on. Allowed values depend on the specified filter dimension.

chevron-rightFilter Values[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#filter-values)

**Offer Type**:

*   `CPR` – Cost Per Registration
    
*   `CPI` - Cost Per Install
    
*   `CPL` – Cost Per Lead
    
*   `CPC` – Cost Per Click
    
*   `CPE` – Cost Per Engagement
    
*   `CPA` – Cost Per Action
    
*   `APK_INSTALL` – APK-based Install
    
*   `APK_REGISTER` – APK-based Registration
    

**Example Curl:**

**Platforms**

*   `ios` – Apple iOS platform
    
*   `android` – Android platform
    
*   `web` – Web-based platform
    

**Example Curl:**

**Country**

*   Countries must be specified using the **standard ISO Alpha-2 country codes** (e.g., `US` for United States, `IN` for India, `FR` for France).
    

**Example Curl:**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#example-response)

Example Response:

chevron-rightResponse Details[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#response-details)

Field

Description

`offers`

An array containing the offer details. Each element represents an individual offer.

`id`

A unique identifier for the offer.

`upd_ts`

The timestamp when the offer was last updated (in UNIX timestamp format).

`off_type`

The type of offer (e.g., `CPI` for Cost Per Install, `CPC` for Cost Per Click, etc.).

`s_id`

The unique identifier for the app associated with the offer.

`name`

The name of the app or offer.

`lp_url`

The link to the landing page for the app (usually a store link).

`pyt`

Payment details for the offer. Contains `cur` (currency) and `amt` (amount).

`inapp_pyt`

Displays payout details in the application's currency, with `cur` representing the currency name and `amt` the amount, based on app settings.

`crtvs`

Creatives related to the offer. Contains `ic_url` (URL to the icon image).

`desc`

Description of the offer. Contains `raw` (raw description text).

`ctg`

Categories associated with the offer (e.g., `SINGLE_STEP`). **Possible values**: `SINGLE_STEP`, `MULTI_REWARD`, `DEPOSIT`, `GAMING`, `FINANCE`, `SURVEY`, `NEW`

`gls`

A list of goals for the offer. Each goal has `id`, `gl_val` (value), `ttl` (title), `instr` (instructions), and `pyt` (payment details) and `inapp_yt`(payment in apps currency).

`trk_url`

Tracking URL for tracking user actions like clicks or installs, with placeholders for dynamic user data.

`geo_tgt`

Geographical targeting information. Contains `include` (countries to include) and `exclude` (countries to exclude).

`os`

The operating system platform for the app (e.g., `android`, `ios`).

`total`

The total number of offers available (in this case, `1931` offers).

`metrics`

Contains performance metrics related to the offer, including CR (Conversion Rate) and EPC (Earnings Per Click). Currently, only global values are supported.

* * *

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#id-3.-click-parameters)

3\. Click Parameters:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use the tracking link provided in the `trk_url` field of each offer in the API response to start sending click events to Pubscale. This tracking link is essential for monitoring user interactions and attributing tasks correctly.

Purpose

The `trk_url` is used to track clicks from users on a particular offer. When a user interacts with an offer, your app or system should trigger this URL with the appropriate parameters.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#supported-click-parameters)

Supported Click Parameters

The following query parameters are supported for integration with the tracking URL:

Parameter

Required

Description

`user_id`

Manadatory

The unique identifier of the user who clicks on the offer. This will be included in the callback. Special characters aren't allowed except "\_","@","-" and ".".

`gaid`

Recomended

Google Advertising ID (required for Android users).

`idfa`

Recomended

Identifier for Advertisers (required for iOS users).

`c1-c5`

Optional

Custom parameters can be appended to the tracking URL by the publisher and will be included in the callback for reference. Special characters aren't allowed except "\_","@","-" and "."

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/api#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

4\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-check

This step is manadatory for rewarding users.

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[PreviousiOSchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/ios)
[NextServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configurationchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

# Sandbox Environment | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

Sandbox environment enables you to test out the integration before you release your app. You will be able to test the complete integration starting from initializing the SDK to getting callbacks.

Also, any changes in the sandbox environment do not affect the production environment.

1.  **Switch to the sandbox environment using the toggle in the dashboard**
    

circle-info

Switching to the Sandbox environment in the dashboard does not affect your production environment.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FNVTUuXGsGT9Ny3shGvow%2FGroup%252078582.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10113b5&sv=2)

Sandbox Environment toggle

1.  **Copy the app ID shown for the sandbox environment and use it in the app**
    
2.  **Additionally, you can also configure a different S2S callback for your sandbox environment by clicking on the Configure Callback button in the sandbox environment.**
    

[PreviousServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configurationchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)
[NextSampleschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/samples)

# Initialize the SDK | 1.0.6-beta2 | Offerwall SDK

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app API key (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

**user\_id:** Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#initializing-the-sdk)

Initializing the SDK

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "APP_ID", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

The SDK Initialization is complete. Learn how to launch the offerwall in the next step.

[PreviousSetting up the SDKchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWallchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/start-the-offerwall)
