# React Native | 1.0.9 | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/react-native#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file

Kotlin Script

Groovy

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.9')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.9'

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/react-native#id-2.-configure-proguard-rules)

2\. Configure proguard rules


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    -keep class com.pubscale.caterpillar.analytics.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/react-native#id-3.-add-native-module-files)

3\. Add native module files


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the following files to your android app's module directory.

*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.javaarrow-up-right](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.java)
    
*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.javaarrow-up-right](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.java)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/react-native#id-3.1.-link-the-module)

3.1. Link the module

Add the following line inside the getPackages() method of MainApplication class.

`packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage());`

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FIIq5KtFCeEF1kXRn81sj%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28a125e0&sv=2)

Adding PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage to React packages

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/react-native#id-4.-initialize-the-sdk)

4\. Initialize the SDK


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app\_id (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

circle-info

Obtain your **app\_id** from the [PubScale Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
 by [adding your app and configuring the offerwall.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
 Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

Parameter

Description

**user\_id**

Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64**

An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64**

An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

# Server-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

circle-info

**Example callback setup:**

**Callback URL set by you:** http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale

**Request sent from us:** HTTP GET http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user\_id=<user\_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>      
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.1.-hash-validation)

3.1. Hash validation

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

PHP

NodeJs

Python

Golang

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

circle-info

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.2.-ip-whitelisting)

3.2. IP Whitelisting

You can restrict the callbacks to be accepted only from our sever IP address(es). Please whitelist the following IP(s) and regularly check back to find possible changes

[PreviousAPIchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api)
[NextSandbox Environmentchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)

*   [1\. Setup Callback URL](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)
    
*   [2\. Server Response](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)
    
*   [3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)
    
*   [3.1. Hash validation](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.1.-hash-validation)
    
*   [Example](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#example)
    
*   [Steps to validate the value of the hash](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)
    
*   [3.2. IP Whitelisting](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.2.-ip-whitelisting)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

Copy

    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            

Copy

    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

Copy

    34.100.236.68

# Web Offerwall | 1.0.9 | Offerwall SDK

triangle-exclamation

Pre-approval from PubScale team is required for Web offerwall integration. Please contact your account manager or reach out to support before starting this integration. [Learn More](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/faqs#how-to-approval-for-web-integration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/web-offerwall#id-1.-integration)

1\. Integration


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1235736282-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%252Fuploads%252FLJHdDEvW1QbJHL6t2Mhj%252FWow_flow%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8ce3cf0-7d40-4a0c-ba09-dba4a24d39b3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b4ec5f5&sv=2)![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1235736282-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%252Fuploads%252Fxw7aKlgdFzQSnMX3ZTEu%252Fwow_flow_dark.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd57ae4fc-140d-4475-b793-7395cacc4527&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=397289b4&sv=2)

To integrate the PubScale Offerwall, you need to provide a set of mandatory parameters for proper configuration.

**Mandatory Parameters**

Parameters

Description

**app\_id**

This is the unique identifier for your app, required for integration.

**user\_id**

A unique identifier for each user, required to track their activity on the offerwall.

To integrate the PubScale Web Offerwall into your website, you have the following options:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/web-offerwall#id-1.1.-using-an-iframe)

**1.1. Using an iframe**:

Place the following iframe in your HTML:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/web-offerwall#id-1.2.-using-a-direct-link)

**1.2. Using a Direct Link**:

Create a direct link to the PubScale Offerwall using an anchor tag. It is recommended to use an image or button for better user experience:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/web-offerwall#id-1.3.-using-javascript)

**1.3. Using JavaScript:**

Open the offerwall link programmatically using `window.open`. This provides flexibility for custom implementations.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/web-offerwall#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/web-offerwall#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

3\. Test the OfferWall


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

To ensure your OfferWall integration is working perfectly, follow these steps during the testing phase.

*   Open the web offerwall and verify that all offers are displayed correctly.
    
*   Complete an offer and confirm that a callback is received from PubScale server to your server. For the sandbox environment, ensure the callback URL is configured properly to receive sandbox callbacks.
    
*   Ensure the hashing technique used matches the one specified in the documentation.
    
*   Verify that the reward value received matches the value displayed for the offer.
    
*   Confirm that the callback is received only from PubScale's [whitelisted server IPs](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)
    .
    

circle-exclamation

While you can use the Web Offerwall in an Android app through a WebView or Custom Chrome Tabs, we have observed better performance and fewer chargebacks when using PubScale's dedicated SDKs. PubScale provides dedicated SDKs for [Android](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration)
, [React Native](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/react-native)
, and [Unity](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity)
, which offer more secure and efficient integration methods. Please consider using these SDKs for better integration.

[PreviousUnitychevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity)
[NextServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configurationchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

Last updated 1 year ago

    const userId = "your_user_id"; // Replace with your unique user ID

# Start the OfferWall | 1.0.6-beta2 | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

Java

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

circle-info

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

Java

[PreviousInitialize the SDKchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk)
[NextSetting up the SDKchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)

Last updated 2 years ago

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallListener offerWallListener = new OfferWallListener() {
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onRewardClaimed(@NonNull Reward reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onFailed(@NonNull String message) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: " + message);
       }
    };

# Unity | 1.0.9 | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#preintegration-checks)

[✅ arrow-up-right](https://www.alt-codes.net/check-mark-symbols.php)
Preintegration checks


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Make sure you are using Unity version 2019.4.0f1 or above
    
*   Ensure your application builds without any errors before adding the plugin.
    
*   Android platform is selected for your Unity project.
    
*   The Editor must support Android Gradle version 4.0.1 or above.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-1.-add-the-offerwall-unity-plugin-to-your-unity-project)

**1\. Add the OfferWall Unity plugin to your Unity project**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Downloadarrow-up-right](https://github.com/GreedyGame/unity-offer_wall_plugin/releases/latest)
 and import the latest version of OfferWall Unity Plugin from GitHub.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-publishing-settings)

**2\. Configuring Publishing Settings**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Set the minimum API level to 24 or above and the target API level to 33 or above under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Other Settings
    
*   Make sure you check the below-mentioned checkboxes under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Publishing Settings.
    
    *   **Custom Main Manifest**
        
    *   **Custom Main Gradle Template**
        
    *   **Custom Gradle Settings Template**
        
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FcdxTWMzbF9XwF5DrIqGX%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25201.06.50%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c388bcc&sv=2)

Player > Publishing settings

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-configuring-dependencies)

**3\. Configuring dependencies**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Adding `mavenCentral()` as a repository in `settingsTemplate.gradle`

Add the below line inside the dependencies block in your mainTemplate.gradle file

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-4.-force-resolve-dependencies)

**4\. Force resolve dependencies**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Force resolve** forces the Package Manager to resolve the project’s packages, reinstalling any altered or missing package and removing extraneous packages.

To Force resolve the dependencies, Goto Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve (if the resolver did not open automatically)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FUzYUObvgE35BpwNoljLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd15261f-4718-4073-ae62-8839fe558896&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c95a673969eca060eea708c9fdc31002608f810ed2f72bebef304fa7c837926b)

Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve

circle-info

OfferWall does not work in the Editor. Please use a real device to test the integration.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-1.-configuring-prefabs)

5\. Configuring Prefabs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#drag-and-drop-pubscaleofferwallobject-prefab)

**Drag and Drop** PubScaleOfferwallObject **prefab**

Drag and drop the **PubScaleOfferwallObject prefab** from Assets/OfferWall/Prefab/PubScaleOfferwallObject.prefab in the scene.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key)

6\. Configuring App Key


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter your PubScale app ID inside the "Pubscale App ID" field located on the PubScaleOfferwallObject.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FpBoMZ7udaVBFv4Ig63fa%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25202.05.03%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ab1a4fc&sv=2)

Offerwall Prefab

circle-info

The PubScale App ID is an 8-digit identifier generated during the app creation process within the dashboard. If you need help creating an account/app with us, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-1)

7\. Initialize the SDK


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To launch the OfferWall, call the PubScaleOfferwallClient.Initialize(string userId) function using the instance from PubScaleOfferwallObject prefab.

circle-info

Expected params:

1.  userID: A string value that is used to identify the user uniquely in your application. If this value is null, the SDK would internally create a userId for the device.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-2)

8\. Custom loader background image and foreground image


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FYnlfddXDB4jW040tGSTw%2FGroup%252078600.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c17efd89&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#step-1-custom-loader-background-and-loader-foreground)

**Step 1: Custom loader background and loader foreground**

To use custom background and foreground images for the loading screen replace the **demo\_background\_img and demo\_foreground\_img** file located under Assets/OfferWall/Resources with the image you need.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#step-2-enable-read-and-write-under-advance-image-settings)

**Step 2: Enable Read and Write under Advance Image settings**

Press the preset button on your imported image and then select the OfferWallTextureImporter preset from the menu and click apply.

circle-info

If the fields are left empty, the default values will be used:

*   Background: Black image
    
*   Foreground: App icon
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-3)

9\. Set Offerwall Orientation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, the Offerwall opens in Portrait orientation. If you want to change this behaviour, do the following changes.

Add the below line inside the <application></application> tag in your AndroidManifest.xml file.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-4)

10\. Handling the SDK callbacks (optional)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To handle the SDK callbacks, subscribe to the events that are made available by the SimpleIntegration script.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-5)

11\. Launch the OfferWall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To launch the OfferWall, call the AdvancedIntegration.ShowOfferWall() function using the PubScaleOfferwallAdvanced prefab.

Can also be used in onClick of a button:

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FST5Hyw2JdLMKSR9Gy8ZO%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25202.09.42%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3052f35&sv=2)

Example usage: Launching Offerwall on click of a button

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

11\. Setup S2S callbacks


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

12\. Test the OfferWall


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

# Android Integration | 1.0.9 | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file. Once added, clean build and rebuild the project.

Kotlin Script

Groovy

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.9')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.9'

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-2.-configure-proguard-rules)

2\. Configure proguard rules


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    
    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    -keep class com.pubscale.caterpillar.analytics.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-initializing-the-offerwall)

3\. Initializing the OfferWall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.1.-parameters-for-init-call)

**3.1. Parameters for init call:**

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.2.-creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**3.2. Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

circle-info

Obtain your **PubScale app ID** from the [PubScale Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
 by [adding your app and configuring the offerwall.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
 Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

Java

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. This can be used in apps or games where an immersive experience is needed. Default: false

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

triangle-exclamation

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.3.-making-the-init-call)

**3.3. Making the init call:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

Java

circle-info

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

circle-info

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-4.-start-the-offerwall)

4\. Start the OfferWall


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

Java

circle-info

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

Java

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

5\. Setup S2S callbacks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

6\. Test the OfferWall


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

# S2S Callback Configuration | 1.0.6-beta1 | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>
          
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

Golang

NodeJs

Python

PHP

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

circle-info

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

[PreviousStart the OfferWallchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/start-the-offerwall)
[NextSandbox Environmentchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [1\. Setup Callback URL](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)
    
*   [2\. Server Response](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)
    
*   [3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)
    

Copy

    
    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

Copy

    
    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    
    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            
        

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

# iOS | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios#id-1.-integration)

1\. Integration


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FLswXTxEAv7IAMykYqwhk%2FWow_flow%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16bc2268&sv=2)![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FpZAkfHGAYoKlDM5kK29m%2Fwow_flow_dark.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b3f2fe3&sv=2)

To integrate the PubScale Offerwall, you need to construct a URL and provide a set of parameters for proper configuration.

**Construct the Offerwall URL**

**Parameters**

Parameters

Description

**app\_id** (Required)

This is the unique identifier for your app, required for integration.

**user\_id** (Required)

A unique identifier for each user, required to track their activity on the offerwall. We recommend using a UUID as the user\_id.

**idfa** (Optional but Recommended)

For iOS integrations Include the **idfa** as a parameter when launching the Offerwall. This helps enhance tracking accuracy and plays a key role in fraud prevention.

To integrate the PubScale Offerwall into your iOS App, you have the following options:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios#using-sfsafariviewcontroller)

Using SFSafariViewController:

For optimal performance and user experience, we recommend launching the Offerwall using `SFSafariViewController`

Here's a simple Swift example that opens PubScale Offerwall in a `SFSafariViewController` on iOS

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios#notes)

Notes:

*   This code should be placed in a `UIViewController` subclass.
    
*   You can call `openLinkInSafariViewController()` when appropriate (e.g., on a button tap or in `viewDidLoad` as shown).
    
*   Don't forget to import `SafariServices`.
    
*   Don't forget to replace the {app\_id} ,{user\_id} and {idfa} with the actula value.
    
*   If your App is not approved from PubScale you might see an error page. ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252FBWTxceAkaguCV1zQT6eh%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-23%2520at%25205.19.10%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81670fb8-3f35-4cf0-8e53-69d5c7a09049&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=deef8c01&sv=2) If you see this error,
    
    *   Check your App ID and make sure it is correct.
        
    *   If your App ID is correct then its possible your App ID is not approved yet, in that case please reach out to your Account Manager to get your App approved.
        
    
    If your configuration is correct, you will see a page similar to the screenshot below. ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252FtgqerDOl95wNtqKZd9FB%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-23%2520at%25205.30.08%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b19efdf-2b9a-4c24-b364-98a0f0f12d48&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b649add7&sv=2)
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

3\. Test the OfferWall


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

To ensure your OfferWall integration is working perfectly, follow these steps during the testing phase.

*   Open the offerwall and verify that all offers are displayed correctly.
    
*   Complete an offer and confirm that a callback is received from PubScale server to your server. For the sandbox environment, ensure the callback URL is configured properly to receive sandbox callbacks.
    
*   Ensure the hashing technique used matches the one specified in the documentation.
    
*   Verify that the reward value received matches the value displayed for the offer.
    
*   Confirm that the callback is received only from PubScale's [whitelisted server IPs](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)
    .
    

[PreviousWebchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web)
[NextAPIchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api)

Last updated 10 months ago

*   [1\. Integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios#id-1.-integration)
    
*   [Using SFSafariViewController:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios#using-sfsafariviewcontroller)
    
*   [2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

Copy

    https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}&idfa={idfa}

Copy

    import UIKit
    import SafariServices
    
    class ViewController: UIViewController {
    
        override func viewDidLoad() {
            super.viewDidLoad()
            openLinkInSafariViewController()
        }
    
        func openLinkInSafariViewController() {
            if let url = URL(string: "https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}&idfa={idfa}") {
                let safariVC = SFSafariViewController(url: url)
                safariVC.modalPresentationStyle = .formSheet
                present(safariVC, animated: true, completion: nil)
            } else {
                print("Invalid URL")
            }
        }
    }

# Start the OfferWall | 1.0.6-beta2 | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `PubscaleOfferwall.launch()` method.

Copy

    PubscaleOfferwall.launch(() => {
        console.log("close"); //onClose
    }, (errMsg) => {
        console.log(errMsg); //onFailure
    });

3\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    
    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    -keep class com.pubscale.caterpillar.analytics.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response

# Setting up your app | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-1.-create-an-account)

1\. Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.comarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-2.-creating-an-offerwall-unit)

2\. Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once you have signed in, you can access Offerwall from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FowcQS6t4xtFB22AF6w1h%2FGroup%252078578.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e14ae4a0&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2Fi95iqP4oFRElNW5IyxRK%2FGroup%252078579.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a819409&sv=2)

1.  Once you’ve created your app in the dashboard and selected the desired integration type (Android SDK, Web Integration, or API), your app will enter a **Pending Approval** state.
    

circle-exclamation

The approval process is **asynchronous** and typically takes **up to 72 hours** as our team manually reviews each submission.

This **does not block your integration** process. We strongly recommend proceeding with the integration immediately. You can use **sandbox mode** to view and test offers while your app is pending approval.

Please make sure to follow the **integration checklist** to ensure you don’t miss any required steps before going live. Once the app is approved, it may take up to 5 minutes for all changes to fully propagate. If you encounter any errors, please wait for 5 minutes after receiving the approval confirmation.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-3.-before-you-go-live)

3\. Before you go live

You can find the checklist by clicking on the **Integration Steps** card

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252FVtWo3URr4olGTGq7nhM4%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-21%2520at%252012.55.22%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daba522d1-0c76-45b8-b386-13c40101e958&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89ce2951&sv=2)

Please make sure you have completed all the steps in the checklist and mark it as completed.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252FCFRw8DRzK9hYYc5lGtCT%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-21%2520at%252012.55.30%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3334727f-bc92-44d9-97aa-ececc4441722&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=733bcb67&sv=2)

# Sandbox Environment | 1.0.6-beta2 | Offerwall SDK

Sandbox environment enables you to test out the integration before you release your app. You will be able to test the complete integration starting from initializing the SDK to getting callbacks.

Also, any changes in the sandbox environment do not affect the production environment.

1.  **Switch to the sandbox environment using the toggle in the dashboard**
    

circle-info

Switching to the Sandbox environment in the dashboard does not affect your production environment.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F47uqFPZw7HlLBl2j2OyM%2Fblobs%2FPS6FBUhu1PWYHkoFILyh%2FGroup%252078582.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ba5a012&sv=2)

Sandbox Environment toggle

1.  **Copy the app ID shown for the sandbox environment and use it in the app**
    
2.  **Additionally, you can also configure a different S2S callback for your sandbox environment by clicking on the Configure Callback button in the sandbox environment.**

# Initialize the SDK | 1.0.6-beta2 | Offerwall SDK

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

Parameters for init call:

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

Java

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
       .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap) //optional
       .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foreground) //optional
       .setFullscreenEnabled(false) //optional
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
                   .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foregroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setFullscreenEnabled(false)//optional
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. Default: false

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

triangle-exclamation

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)

**Initialize the Offerwall SDK:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

Java

circle-info

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

circle-info

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

[PreviousSetting up the SDKchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWallchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/start-the-offerwall)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [Creating OfferWallConfig object:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)
    
*   [](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)
    
*   [Initialize the Offerwall SDK:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)
    

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, object : OfferWallInitListener {
       override fun onInitSuccess() {
       }
       override fun onInitFailed(error: InitError) {
       }
    })

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, new OfferWallInitListener() {
       @Override
       public void onInitSuccess() {
    
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onInitFailed(@NonNull InitError error) {
    
       }
    });

# React Native | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file

Kotlin Script

Groovy

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.10')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.10'

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-2.-configure-proguard-rules)

2\. Configure proguard rules


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    -keep class com.pubscale.caterpillar.analytics.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-3.-add-native-module-files)

3\. Add native module files


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the following files to your android app's module directory.

*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.javaarrow-up-right](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.java)
    
*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.javaarrow-up-right](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.java)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-3.1.-link-the-module)

3.1. Link the module

Add the following line inside the getPackages() method of MainApplication class.

`packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage());`

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FyOsGnn7xvrwAZswYQNh1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77cf04c&sv=2)

Adding PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage to React packages

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-4.-initialize-the-sdk)

4\. Initialize the SDK


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app\_id (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

circle-info

Obtain your **app\_id** from the [PubScale Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
 by [adding your app and configuring the offerwall.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
 Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

Parameter

Description

**user\_id**

Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64**

An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64**

An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-4.1.-making-the-init-call)

4.1. Making the Init call

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-5.-start-the-offerwall)

5\. Start the OfferWall


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start the offerwall, just call, `PubscaleOfferwall.launch()` method.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

6\. Setup S2S callbacks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

7\. Test the OfferWall


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "app_id", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

Copy

    PubscaleOfferwall.launch(() => {
        console.log("close"); //onClose
    }, (errMsg) => {
        console.log(errMsg); //onFailure
    });

# S2S Callback Configuration | 1.0.6-beta2 | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>
          
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

Golang

NodeJs

Python

PHP

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

circle-info

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

[PreviousStart the OfferWallchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/start-the-offerwall)
[NextIP Whitelistchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [1\. Setup Callback URL](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)
    
*   [2\. Server Response](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)
    
*   [3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)
    

Copy

    
    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

Copy

    
    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    
    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            
        

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

# Web | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-1.-integration)

1\. Integration


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

circle-info

You can download the Sample integration from [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/GreedyGame/demo-offerwall-web)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FLswXTxEAv7IAMykYqwhk%2FWow_flow%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16bc2268&sv=2)![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FpZAkfHGAYoKlDM5kK29m%2Fwow_flow_dark.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b3f2fe3&sv=2)

To integrate the PubScale Offerwall, you need to provide a set of mandatory parameters for proper configuration.

**Parameters**

Parameters

Description

**app\_id** (Required)

This is the unique identifier for your app, required for integration.

**user\_id** (Required)

A unique identifier for each user, required to track their activity on the offerwall. We recommend using a UUID as the user\_id.

**idfa** (Optional)

For iOS integrations Include the **idfa** as a parameter when launching the Web Offerwall. This helps enhance tracking accuracy and plays a key role in fraud prevention.

**ga\_id** (Optional)

For Android integrations Include the **ga\_id** as a parameter when launching the Web Offerwall. This helps enhance tracking accuracy and plays a key role in fraud prevention.

To integrate the PubScale Web Offerwall into your website, you have the following options:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-1.1.-using-an-iframe)

**1.1. Using an iframe**:

Place the following iframe in your HTML:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-1.2.-using-a-direct-link)

**1.2. Using a Direct Link**:

Create a direct link to the PubScale Offerwall using an anchor tag. It is recommended to use an image or button for better user experience:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-1.3.-using-javascript)

**1.3. Using JavaScript:**

Open the offerwall link programmatically using `window.open`. This provides flexibility for custom implementations.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

3\. Test the OfferWall


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

To ensure your OfferWall integration is working perfectly, follow these steps during the testing phase.

*   Open the web offerwall and verify that all offers are displayed correctly.
    
*   Complete an offer and confirm that a callback is received from PubScale server to your server. For the sandbox environment, ensure the callback URL is configured properly to receive sandbox callbacks.
    
*   Ensure the hashing technique used matches the one specified in the documentation.
    
*   Verify that the reward value received matches the value displayed for the offer.
    
*   Confirm that the callback is received only from PubScale's [whitelisted server IPs](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)
    .
    

circle-exclamation

While you can use the Web Offerwall in an Android app through a WebView or Custom Chrome Tabs, we have observed better performance and fewer chargebacks when using PubScale's dedicated SDKs. PubScale provides dedicated SDKs for [Android](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration)
, [React Native](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native)
, and [Unity](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity)
, which offer more secure and efficient integration methods. Please consider using these SDKs for better integration.

[PreviousUnitychevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity)
[NextiOSchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios)
