# Unity | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#preintegration-checks)

[✅ arrow-up-right](https://www.alt-codes.net/check-mark-symbols.php)
Preintegration checks


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Make sure you are using Unity version 2019.4.0f1 or above
    
*   Ensure your application builds without any errors before adding the plugin.
    
*   Android platform is selected for your Unity project.
    
*   The Editor must support Android Gradle version 4.0.1 or above.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-1.-add-the-offerwall-unity-plugin-to-your-unity-project)

**1\. Add the OfferWall Unity plugin to your Unity project**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Downloadarrow-up-right](https://github.com/GreedyGame/unity-offer_wall_plugin/releases/latest)
 and import the latest version of OfferWall Unity Plugin from GitHub.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-publishing-settings)

**2\. Configuring Publishing Settings**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Set the minimum API level to 24 or above and the target API level to 33 or above under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Other Settings
    
*   Make sure you check the below-mentioned checkboxes under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Publishing Settings.
    
    *   **Custom Main Manifest**
        
    *   **Custom Main Gradle Template**
        
    *   **Custom Gradle Settings Template**
        
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2Fs8TJG5WoN6GOK95xrVXr%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25201.06.50%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c877c055&sv=2)

Player > Publishing settings

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-configuring-dependencies)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Adding `mavenCentral()` as a repository in `settingsTemplate.gradle`

Add the below line inside the dependencies block in your mainTemplate.gradle file

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-4.-force-resolve-dependencies)

**4\. Force resolve dependencies**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Force resolve** forces the Package Manager to resolve the project’s packages, reinstalling any altered or missing package and removing extraneous packages.

To Force resolve the dependencies, Goto Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve (if the resolver did not open automatically)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FUzYUObvgE35BpwNoljLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd15261f-4718-4073-ae62-8839fe558896&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c95a673969eca060eea708c9fdc31002608f810ed2f72bebef304fa7c837926b)

# Android Integration | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

circle-exclamation

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

circle-info

You can download the Sample integration from [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/greedygame/demo-offerwall-android)

[https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Qngthh24lsEwww.youtube.comchevron-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Qngthh24lsE)

Offerwall Android SDK integration video tutorial

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file. Once added, clean build and rebuild the project.

Kotlin Script

Groovy

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-2.-configure-proguard-rules)

2\. Configure proguard rules


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-initializing-the-offerwall)

3\. Initializing the OfferWall


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.1.-parameters-for-init-call)

**3.1. Parameters for init call:**

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.2.-creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**3.2. Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

circle-info

Obtain your **PubScale app ID** from the [PubScale Dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
 by [adding your app and configuring the offerwall.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
 Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

circle-info

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

Java

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. This can be used in apps or games where an immersive experience is needed. Default: false

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

triangle-exclamation

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.3.-making-the-init-call)

**3.3. Making the init call:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

Java

circle-exclamation

Make sure to handle Offerwall init failures properly as the init might fail in scenarios where the PubScale system detects a fraudulent environment.

circle-info

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-4.-start-the-offerwall)

4\. Start the OfferWall


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

Java

circle-info

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

Java

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

5\. Setup S2S callbacks


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

6\. Test the OfferWall


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

# API | 1.0.10 | Offerwall SDK

By integrating this API, publishers can seamlessly fetch and display these offers within their own user interface. This allows for the creation of fully native and personalised in-app experiences that align with the app’s design and user flow, enhancing user engagement and improving conversion rates.

triangle-exclamation

Pre-approval from PubScale team is required for the offerwall integration. Please contact your account manager or reach out to support before starting this integration. [Learn More](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/faqs#how-to-approval-for-web-integration)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#id-1.-authentication)

1\. Authentication


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to access offers API. Following Keys need to be generated.

1.  Pub Key (Generated once per publisher)
    
2.  App ID
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#app-id)

App-ID

In order to generate an App ID follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit App ID. This will be used as App ID to access the API.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#pub-key)

Pub-Key

In order the generate a Publisher Key a pre-approval is required. This is a one time approval for a publisher. Please contact account manager for the same.

After your account is approved, you can proceed with the following steps to generate your Publisher API Key.

triangle-exclamation

**When you regenerate the Offerwall API Key, the new key will apply to all apps linked to your account.**

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#steps)

Steps:

1.  Once logged in, you’ll find Settings in the side navigation panel.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252FLzR9y0rl7Ktqmh2mp8M9%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5672c74a-5251-410b-b997-63b0923f68b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=364ee0ea&sv=2)

1.  Go to the API Key section to generate your Offerwall API key. If you don't see this section, please contact your account manager for enabling access.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252Fvvxyxxm8IhUk6EukFbVo%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D734fde72-9169-4094-8dba-2ee7d627240c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a21ec49e&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to the Offerwall API section to access and create your Offerwall API key.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252F9LbRADkCv47wyFGAK56w%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5c01bb9-6363-4e37-bbb2-38469aa8a75f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d6ad453&sv=2)

1.  Please copy the key from the image and paste it into your Offerwall API setup.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252FkLx6pyQz5jerPC0XG5O4%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e6db12f-36ad-4005-9fed-d6e897764e38&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8cad21e3&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#id-2.-offers-api)

2\. Offers API:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#description)

Description:

The API provides a list of offers available for your app, which can be used to display and run offers on your platform.

circle-exclamation

Offers are cached on our server and refreshed every 5 minutes. We recommend updating your inventory accordingly.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#endpoint)

Endpoint:

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#auth)

Auth:

The keys generated in the previous steps must be included in the following headers when making API requests.

These are **Mandatory** for accessing the API.

*   **App-Id** – The unique App ID generated for your app during the setup process.
    
*   **Pub-Key** – The unique key generated for your publisher account during setup. This key is shared across all apps within the same account.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#example)

Example:

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#payload)

Payload:

Body

Required

Type

Description

page

Required

Integer

The `page` field in the Offers API response indicates the current page number and should always be a positive integer.

size

Required

Integer

The `size` field in the Offers API response represents the number of offers returned in that response and should always be a positive integer.

filt

Optional

Array

Contains an array of filters to be applied to the Offers API request to refine the results based on specified criteria.

dim

Optional

String

Specifies the dimension on which the filter is applied. Supported values are `offer_type`, `platform`, and `country`.

match

Optional

Model

Contains details about the filter to be applied, including the values to filter by and the match type used for filtering.

type

Optional

String

Specifies the match type to be used for the filter. Supported values are `any` (matches any of the provided values) and `exact` (requires a single, exact value match).

values

Optional

Array

Contains the values to apply the filter on. Allowed values depend on the specified filter dimension.

chevron-rightFilter Values[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#filter-values)

**Offer Type**:

*   `CPR` – Cost Per Registration
    
*   `CPI` - Cost Per Install
    
*   `CPL` – Cost Per Lead
    
*   `CPC` – Cost Per Click
    
*   `CPE` – Cost Per Engagement
    
*   `CPA` – Cost Per Action
    
*   `APK_INSTALL` – APK-based Install
    
*   `APK_REGISTER` – APK-based Registration
    

**Example Curl:**

**Platforms**

*   `ios` – Apple iOS platform
    
*   `android` – Android platform
    
*   `web` – Web-based platform
    

**Example Curl:**

**Country**

*   Countries must be specified using the **standard ISO Alpha-2 country codes** (e.g., `US` for United States, `IN` for India, `FR` for France).
    

**Example Curl:**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#example-response)

Example Response:

chevron-rightResponse Details[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#response-details)

Field

Description

`offers`

An array containing the offer details. Each element represents an individual offer.

`id`

A unique identifier for the offer.

`upd_ts`

The timestamp when the offer was last updated (in UNIX timestamp format).

`off_type`

The type of offer (e.g., `CPI` for Cost Per Install, `CPC` for Cost Per Click, etc.).

`s_id`

The unique identifier for the app associated with the offer.

`name`

The name of the app or offer.

`lp_url`

The link to the landing page for the app (usually a store link).

`pyt`

Payment details for the offer. Contains `cur` (currency) and `amt` (amount).

`inapp_pyt`

Displays payout details in the application's currency, with `cur` representing the currency name and `amt` the amount, based on app settings.

`crtvs`

Creatives related to the offer. Contains `ic_url` (URL to the icon image).

`desc`

Description of the offer. Contains `raw` (raw description text).

`ctg`

Categories associated with the offer (e.g., `SINGLE_STEP`). **Possible values**: `SINGLE_STEP`, `MULTI_REWARD`, `DEPOSIT`, `GAMING`, `FINANCE`, `SURVEY`, `NEW`

`gls`

A list of goals for the offer. Each goal has `id`, `gl_val` (value), `ttl` (title), `instr` (instructions), and `pyt` (payment details) and `inapp_yt`(payment in apps currency).

`trk_url`

Tracking URL for tracking user actions like clicks or installs, with placeholders for dynamic user data.

`geo_tgt`

Geographical targeting information. Contains `include` (countries to include) and `exclude` (countries to exclude).

`os`

The operating system platform for the app (e.g., `android`, `ios`).

`total`

The total number of offers available (in this case, `1931` offers).

`metrics`

Contains performance metrics related to the offer, including CR (Conversion Rate) and EPC (Earnings Per Click). Currently, only global values are supported.

* * *

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#id-3.-click-parameters)

3\. Click Parameters:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use the tracking link provided in the `trk_url` field of each offer in the API response to start sending click events to Pubscale. This tracking link is essential for monitoring user interactions and attributing tasks correctly.

Purpose

The `trk_url` is used to track clicks from users on a particular offer. When a user interacts with an offer, your app or system should trigger this URL with the appropriate parameters.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#supported-click-parameters)

Supported Click Parameters

The following query parameters are supported for integration with the tracking URL:

Parameter

Required

Description

`user_id`

Manadatory

The unique identifier of the user who clicks on the offer. This will be included in the callback. Special characters aren't allowed except "\_","@","-" and ".".

`gaid`

Recomended

Google Advertising ID (required for Android users).

`idfa`

Recomended

Identifier for Advertisers (required for iOS users).

`c1-c5`

Optional

Custom parameters can be appended to the tracking URL by the publisher and will be included in the callback for reference. Special characters aren't allowed except "\_","@","-" and "."

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

4\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-check

This step is manadatory for rewarding users.

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[PreviousiOSchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios)
[NextServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configurationchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

Last updated 9 months ago

# Welcome to Immersive Ads 2 | Immersive Ads SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FVmnIa0j6JrCbyVHQR8lO%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e5b12c06&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Immersive Ads SDK is a powerful tool that enables developers to seamlessly integrate native ads into their Unity mobile games.

With this SDK, developers can monetize their games by displaying non-intrusive native ads in the game scenes, providing players with an engaging advertising experience.

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk#features)

Features


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Easy Drag & Drop integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done entirely without touching code.
    
2.  **Native Ad Display Prefabs:** Ready-to-use ad prefabs that dynamically adjust themselves based on different dimensions of ad creatives received from Advertisers.
    
3.  **Boost Revenue:** Earn recurring incremental revenue with a one-time integration process.
    
4.  **Scripting API:** You also have the option of using the Scripting API to trigger ad events from code.
    
5.  **Dynamic Configuration:** Change and fine-tune ad behavior on the go after publishing with our remote config features.
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk#quick-links)

Quick links


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboardarrow-up-right](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [SDK Github pagearrow-up-right](https://github.com/GreedyGame/immersive-ads-unity)
    

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk#get-started)

Get Started


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides to set up our SDK quickly and easily.

[📪Prerequisiteschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/prerequisites/prerequisites)

# Adding the SDK | Immersive Ads SDK

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/adding-the-sdk#id-1.-add-the-google-mobile-a-ds-plugin-to-your-project)

1\. Add the Google Mobile Ads plugin to your project

[Downloadarrow-up-right](https://github.com/googleads/googleads-mobile-unity/releases)
 and import the **Google Mobile Ads** **plugin.**

Note: The SDK supports AdMob version **v9.6.0 and upwards**

**2\. Add the PubScale Immersive Ads 2 plugin to your project**

Contact your Account Manager to obtain the SDK package. Import the package into your project.

**3\. Ensuring 16KB page size compliance on Android**

*   If upgrading from a previous version of the SDK (2.1.0 or earlier), make sure to delete the GoogleMobileAdsNative folder and re-import from the latest SDK package.
    
*   Failing to do so will not result in errors; however, the app will fail to run on a device with a 16 KB memory page size, and the AAB file will be flagged on the Play Console for containing 16 KB incompatible libraries.
    

**4\. Force Resolve Dependencies**

Force resolve the dependencies from **Assets/External Dependency Manager/Android Resolver/Force Resolve** if the resolver did not open automatically.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2Fk2ItUpE5zm3uRntohTwf%2FforceResolve.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e96157fe&sv=2)

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to link the app in the next step.

[PreviousDemand Source setupchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/prerequisites/demand-source-setup)
[NextApp Linkingchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/app-linking)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Testing the integration | Immersive Ads SDK

To test the integration, always check the **Use Test Mode** **field in the** PubScale Editor window. This will enable test ads and show a debug UI over the native ad for checking Ad Impressions and Clicks.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2443726033-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%252Fuploads%252FYku5NgUXXt2ccizxS0PZ%252FEnable%2520Test%2520mode.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d36034d-658f-443d-81bb-6c3de321fc24&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=971c7828&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/testing-the-integration#editor-test-a-ds)

**Editor Test Ads**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hit the play button in the editor and ensure editor test ads are visible and there are no errors or warnings.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/testing-the-integration#test-impressions-and-clicks)

**Test Impressions and clicks**

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/testing-the-integration#checking-viewability-in-editor)

**Checking Viewability in Editor**

You can get an estimated feedback for impression viewability in the Editor itself using the status visualizer, as shown in the video.

circle-info

Note: The Unity editor is not a production environment. The editor's feedback may not be 100% accurate in all cases, and a final check should be done on an actual device.

This step should be used as a time-saving tool when adding ad placements to the game scenes. The final check for impressions and clickability should be done on a device, as described in the next section.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/testing-the-integration#testing-on-device)

**Testing on Device**

Finally, to test Impressions and Clicks, **build the application on an actual device****.** Check if you can see the impression indicator turning green when the ad comes inside the camera view, and the click indicator turning green when you tap on the ad.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FZ10Uf08hiX78ox9D66E8%2FTest%2520Ad%25201.jpg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1734cd3c&sv=2)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2Fat84vorEuHzWCsktj8Dm%2FTest%2520Ad%25202.jpg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6c841ff&sv=2)

[PreviousScene setupchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/scene-setup)
[NextIntegration Checklistchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist)

# Prerequisites | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/prerequisites/prerequisites#before-starting-the-sdk-integration-make-a-quick-check-of-the-things-listed-below)

Before starting the SDK integration, make a quick check of the things listed below:

1.  Make sure you are using Unity version 2021.3.45f2 and upwards
    
2.  The platform selected for your Unity project is based on the target device
    
3.  You have the GAM App ID or [AdMob app IDarrow-up-right](https://admob.google.com/home/)
     and a Google IIG (Immersive in-game) ad unit ID. Make sure the AdMob Unity SDK version is **v9.6.0 or above**
    
4.  You have a [PubScale App ID](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/prerequisites/demand-source-setup)
     for the platform you are targeting (Android / iOS)
    
5.  Ensure your application builds without any errors BEFORE adding the SDK
    

* * *

**GAM DEMAND SET UP WITH PUBSCALE:**

*   Get in touch with your Account Manager to complete the demand setup.
    

**IF YOU HAVE ACCESS TO GOOGLE IMMERSIVE ON ADMOB:**

*   Share the Admob App ID and Admob Google IIG Ad unit ID with your AM
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2F68ax5FTpu8HAf8WVn9nC%2FIIG%2520Unit%2520Creation.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c456ad8&sv=2)

# Ad Object Structure | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/ad-object-structure#a-d-image-components-in-the-admob-native-ad-format)

**AD IMAGE COMPONENTS IN THE ADMOB NATIVE AD FORMAT**

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FMDZWs4uf7sfGdXZ3pMeW%2FScreenshot_20231201_163049.jpg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65060052&sv=2)

1.  Small icon image (e.g. advertiser logo)
    
2.  The Big image showing the product
    

*   The Ad fill may or may not have a big product image.
    
*   If the big product image is available, it can be of landscape, square, or portrait aspect ratio.
    
*   The SDK handles all these conditions automatically and contains Display Handler Templates for the different cases.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/ad-object-structure#id-1.1-understanding-the-a-d-display-variants)

1.1 **UNDERSTANDING THE AD DISPLAY VARIANTS**

The Display Handling Templates can be broadly classified under two categories:

1.  MEDIA VIEW TYPES (Ad contains Big Image)
    
    1.  MediaLandscapeSimple
        
    2.  MediaLanscapeBlur
        
    3.  MediaPortrait
        
    
2.  NON MEDIA VIEW (Ad does not contain Big Image)
    
    1.  NonMedia
        
    

* * *

**1.2 STRUCTURE OF THE SDK AD PREFAB**

The structure of SDK's Ad object is shown below:

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FgXMYoTV5yye8Zn3gFqBe%2FStructure%2520of%2520Ad%2520object.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edd708c6&sv=2)

The object hierarchy is similar for both Screen Space (SS\_NativeAd) and World Space (WS\_NativeAd) with minor differences

OBJECT NAME

DESCRIPTION

Placeholder

An image to show before the Ad loads This can also be set to None or 100% transparent to show nothing before the Ad is loaded

MediaViewTypes

Parent for all Display Templates containing Big Image

NonMediaView

Parent for Display Templates without Big Image

StatusVisualiser

A debug tool that indicates impression and click detection status Only displayed with Test ads

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/ad-object-structure#id-1.3-general-structure-of-display-handler-template-objects)

**1.3 GENERAL STRUCTURE OF DISPLAY HANDLER TEMPLATE OBJECTS**

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2Fyr92T7K0fKu4ZM5Yz77a%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-03%2520at%252011.44.54%2520PM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47885f2d&sv=2)

The image above shows the object hierarchy of the MediaLandscapeSimple display template. The structure is similar to other templates as well with minor variations.

GameObject NAME

DESCRIPTION

BigImage

Has image component to display Big Product texture

AdIconImageHolder

Background for Ad Icon

AdIconImg

Has image component to display Advertiser Logo icon

# Troubleshoot | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-6ebe3b5a-e6da-4390-b370-a348944ef7e3)

Ad Loading Failed

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2Fsml8WQsbZovwGomcKxF6%2FScreenshot_20240205-145155.jpg&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=84af6e89&sv=2)

1.  Make sure you have added the App ID inside the Google AdMob settings window.
    
2.  In the case of live ad ID (Test mode off), this may happen if there is no fill from the Google server.
    
3.  You may encounter this issue when using Unity Editor Version 2021 or later with AdMob versions 9.6.0 or above. To fix this, ensure that you are building your application with IL2CPP as the scripting backend.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-75d19063-242b-486e-b874-ed3aeb011c24)

No Impressions

1.  If the screen-space ad unit does not receive impressions
    
    1.  It may be due to a low resize scale. Increase the ad unit’s resize scale to ensure it is visible.
        
    2.  If you’re using Screen space - camera render mode for SS ad unit, instead, you can directly use overlay canvas render mode.
        
    
2.  In dynamic 3D game environments, a world-space ad unit may not receive impressions if it is positioned too far from the camera, partially outside the camera’s viewport, or sized too small. Ensure the ad unit is completely visible, meets viewability pixel requirements, and has an adequate resize scale to satisfy viewing angle and screen coverage criteria.
    

1.  It's important to understand how ad impressions are measured. Impressions are counted based on the IAB's Intrinsic In-Game Advertising Guidelines, which require an ad to meet both a minimum pixel and time-on-screen threshold.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#impression_measurement_standards)

Impression Measurement Industry Standards

The minimum criteria for a viewable ad impression are:

*   **Display Ads**: At least 50% of the ad's pixels are on screen for a continuous period of at least one second.
    
*   **Video Ads**: At least 50% of the ad's pixels are on screen for a continuous period of at least two seconds. This does not need to be the first two seconds of the video.
    

While it can be challenging to follow these guidelines throughout an entire gameplay session, they should be a key consideration when designing specific ad placements that players will encounter during planned moments in your game.

1.  Make sure there is no collider between the main camera and the ad Unit.
    
2.  Make sure the Unity Event system component is present in the scene.
    
3.  If you are instantiating ad prefabs in real-time, try disabling the strip engine code option from the build option.
    
    ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FnRTulXK1XDYkvKSf6utW%2Ftroubleshooting-1.20b9f76e01fde8dfc365.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b082c48c&sv=2)
    

1.  If you have multiple cameras on the scene. There are 2 options to address:
    
    1.  Make sure the camera that is looking toward the ad unit has the highest priority depth value.
        
    2.  Use the [**SetActiveCameraForMeasurement**](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#static-methods)
         on PubScaleManager to set a specific camera to be used for impression check.
        
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2Fv6zmnqr12NX3UUdPnLg9%2Ftroubleshooting-2.b59384c8cc7c6ab8674a.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=704e3803&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-87812b65-8d1a-4fe4-adb0-06debb085501)

Impression but No Click

1.  Make sure there is no collider between the main camera and the ad Unit.
    
2.  For persistent on-screen UI, you can register UI GameObjects that the SDK will ignore as obstructions when the user clicks on an ad in the game to click through using the PubScaleManager [RegisterFriendlyObstruction](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#static-methods)
     API
    
3.  Make sure the Unity Event system component is present in the scene.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-87812b65-8d1a-4fe4-adb0-06debb085501-1)

The game audio goes mute when there is a video ad fill

*   Check if Mute Other Audio Source is enabled
    
*   To prevent this behaviour, uncheck Mute Other Audio Sources in Player Settings > Other Settings
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FasK4SOBVCAGBA6cZbP5a%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c954a712&sv=2)

[PreviousIntegration Checklistchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist)
[NextImportant Changeschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes)

*   [No Impressions](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-75d19063-242b-486e-b874-ed3aeb011c24)

# Important Changes | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes#industry-in-transition)

INDUSTRY IN TRANSITION

*   As the in-game native ads industry matures, the delivery of native ads is changing as well.
    

*   It's moving away from needing to assemble each element of the ad (heading text, logo image, big image, star rating, etc ) on the client side by the developer to the Demand partners providing the composed ad creative image or video ready to display in the game.
    

*   While there is a certain trade-off in creative control in the new direction, it enables better ad measurements, higher revenues due to increased advertiser trust.
    

**AD SHAPE**

A step in this direction is moving towards standardised native ad aspect ratios (Ad shapes). The SDK refers to these aspect ratios as **Fixed Aspect Ratio** **Ads**.

List of currently supported Fixed aspect ratios:

*   1x1
    
*   6x5
    
*   32x10
    

The aspect ratio can be viewed in the NativeAdDisplayHandler inspector. A single Ad object can support the display of multiple aspect ratios.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2443726033-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%252Fuploads%252FgWSewGAxFcD94p2MzJnz%252FAdAspectRatio%2520Highlight%2520v260.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D601ef70b-a299-4a2b-a604-9d99beaba568&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9ec47589&sv=2)

**AD SPACE**

In addition to Ad Aspect Ratio, another important detail is the Ad Space - whether it is part of the UI (**Canvas**) or the game world (**World**).

circle-info

Ad Space is auto-detected by the SDK and does not need to be manually set in the NativeAdDisplayHandler

* * *

A majority of the demand in the new version of the SDK will serve ads delivered under the new mechanism and requires 3 simple steps for ad display customisation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes#id-1.-adjust-the-a-d-resize-scale-in-nativeadholder)

**1\.** **Adjust the AD Resize Scale in NativeAdHolder**

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2Fb5LRrCK6JWXGFZNl4gj7%2FNAH%2520Updated.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50502cdb&sv=2)

**Select a scale factor that best fits the ad within the available ad space.** \***CUSTOM RESIZE SCALE OVERRIDE:**

If the NativeAdHolder supports multiple aspect ratios, you can override the scale of a specific aspect ratio in its NativeAdDisplayHandler component inspector to get a more precise fit. For instance, here is an example of a custom scale override applied to 1x1 Display Handler.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2443726033-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%252Fuploads%252FS6h5j09yrNxLAGnurkyw%252FCustom%2520Scale%2520Override%2520Green%25201x1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60395564-3877-45af-8867-248ab2dde9a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2653e80b&sv=2)

You can test an ad size in the Editor Play mode to get the best fit inside the Ad space

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FPa5AO1wDmcG7zD6eCGuH%2FOverlap%2520Visual%2520Check.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a73cccb2&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes#id-2.-assign-a-creative-to-the-a-d-frame-to-make-it-stand-out)

**2\. Assign a creative to the ad frame to make it stand out**

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FS0SpUMoIR81Pc9Hz9kdb%2Fad%2520frame%25201.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e7516b&sv=2) ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FWHcitdLucIOXuSGXgu9R%2Fad%2520frame%25202.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2203823a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes#id-3.-adjust-a-d-badge-for-better-ad-policy-compliance)

**3\. Adjust Ad Badge for better ad policy compliance**

It is important to have the ad badge clearly visible and inform the user that they are viewing an ad. You can customize the ad badge placement and image sprite as shown below.

\***CUSTOM AD BADGE OVERRIDE:**

Similar to applying a custom resize scale override as shown above, a custom Ad badge can be assigned in the NativeAdDisplayHandler inspector.

This is useful for cases where the supported Aspect ratio vary significantly in shape (for example, 1x1 and 32x10). In this case, a custom ad badge placed at more suitable position can be assigned for the specific aspect ratio.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2443726033-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%252Fuploads%252FSABL9BzT4IwehYp7DecD%252FCustom%2520Ad%2520Badge.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbfd606ba-f3e0-4dbf-9546-21cf524826d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=413d87a5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes#customizations-for-demand-in-custom-aspect-formats)

CUSTOMIZATIONS FOR DEMAND IN CUSTOM ASPECT FORMATS

*   A section of the demand will still be received in the custom aspect ratio formats. While it's optional, you can follow the steps provided in the next 3 sections to customize the look of ad display objects, which render demand received in the old format (individual ad elements).
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2F2PU8KpiJ8e7EJ99R2X6k%2Fhttps___content.gitbook.com_content_Ti7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um_blobs_ztV66RLxgWzTtHxCA2ZT_Screenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25208.14.41%2520PM.avif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc72e6e0&sv=2)

# Scene setup | Immersive Ads SDK

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/scene-setup#id-1.-configure-pubscalemanager-prefab)

**1\. Configure PubScaleManager prefab**

Drag and drop the PubScaleManager prefab from **Assets/PubscaleSDK/Common/Prefabs/PubScaleManager.prefab** in the first scene in your Build Settings.

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/scene-setup#id-2.-drag-and-drop-native-a-d-unit-prefab)

2\. Drag and Drop Native Ad Unit prefab

Drag and drop any of the Native ad unit prefab from the path Assets > PubScaleSDK > NativeAds > Prefabs > AdHolderUnits into your gameplay scene.

circle-info

If using any prefab from the “ScreenSpaceCamera” folder, then put it under a Canvas using **Screen Space-Camera** render or **Overlay render mode.**

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/scene-setup#id-3.-assign-unique-a-d-tag-for-ad-units)

**3\. Assign Unique Ad Tag for Ad Units**

Ensure each ad unit has a unique Ad Tag assigned. Example: Home\_Screen\_Unit or level\_fail\_ad\_unit. This allows us to analyze the performance of each ad unit for further optimization.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FlN5jlFc0U9saiRuHELUZ%2FAdTag.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f6d64b4&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/scene-setup#id-4.-set-the-first-a-d-request-details)

**4\. Set the First Ad Request Details**

A new option added from v2.6.0 of the SDK gives you control over the initial caching behaviour depending on the first ad placement in your game and aspect ratio it supports (See - PRESENTATION > Important Changes section for more details)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2443726033-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%252Fuploads%252FnCVoSG2SSaevRwvH4pe6%252FFirst%2520Ad%2520Request.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D933cc01f-c750-4f3a-848f-b8aa8a3730e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4a78c43&sv=2)

You can set the aspect ratio and space of the First Ad you want the SDK to cache in the PubScale Window Settings. This ensures the the right type of ad is requested by the time the first ad placement in the game is shown to the user.

We have now completed setting up the ads. Let's proceed to the next step to learn how to test the ads.

[NextTesting the integrationchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/testing-the-integration)

# PubScaleManager | Immersive Ads SDK

The PubScaleManager handles initialization and all the requests and response caching for ads. It is a singleton component that can be accessed from anywhere. Native ads won't work if this component is missing from the scene.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#properties)

Properties

Name

Description

**IsInitialized**

Use to check if the PubScale SDK is initialized

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#static-methods)

Static Methods

Name

Description

SetActiveCameraForMeasurement

By default, the SDK uses the camera with the highest depth for measurement. In scenes with multiple cameras, this default camera might not be the one rendering the primary game screen from the player's perspective.

If the wrong camera is used for measurement, the SDK cannot determine if the ad is viewable, which prevents impressions from being reported. It can also cause the ad to be unclickable.

Use this method to explicitly set the camera that is aligned with the player's view

SetSdkToRemoveAdsPurchasedForThisSession

Use this API to adjust SDKs behaviour when Remove Ads IAP is active for a session. The SDK does not persist this information as Remove Ads can be permanent or part of a time based subscription. This API needs to be set on app open every session when RemoveAds is active

RegisterFriendlyObstruction

You can register up to 2 UI GameObjects that the SDK will ignore as obstructions when the user clicks on an ad in the game with the intention of clicking through. A friendly UI object example could be a virtual joystick that appears on the screen wherever the user taps.

UnRegisterFriendlyObstruction

Use this method to un-register a UI gameobject previously registered as a friendly object. When switching scenes, you must call `UnRegisterFriendlyObstruction()` before the API call to load the new scene, instead of doing it in `OnDestroy()` . This ensures proper cleanup and prevents issues when switching scenes.

[PreviousExtra Display Templateschevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates)
[NextNativeAdHolderchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Properties](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#properties)
    
*   [Static Methods](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#static-methods)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Integration Checklist | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#basic-checks)

Basic Checks:

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-1.-replace-the-pubscale-placeholder)

1\. **Replace the PubScale Placeholder**

It is important that you replace the PubScale placeholder with your game’s assets, which is displayed when there's no ad available.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2F1IJJihxNCEK7Ji31vpCh%2FPlaceholder1.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bde3f2a8&sv=2)

2\. **Assign Unique Ad Tag for Ad Units**

Ensure each ad unit has a unique Ad Tag assigned. Example: Home\_Screen\_Unit or level\_fail\_ad\_unit. This allows us to analyze the performance of each ad unit for further optimization.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FlN5jlFc0U9saiRuHELUZ%2FAdTag.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f6d64b4&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#visual-checks)

Visual Checks:

1\. **Avoid Ad Unit Overlap with Screen Elements**

Ensure ad units do not overlap with other on-screen elements.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FQbYtiE7OIW9yHGpjFWIg%2FAdUnit%2520Overlap.gif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=51bd0ba5&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#functional-checks)

Functional Checks:

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-1.-ensure-impressions-and-clicks-are-registered)

1\. **Ensure Impressions and Clicks are registered**

Build the application to an actual device. Verify if the impression indicator turns green when the ad is in the camera view and if the click indicator turns green when you tap on the ad.

circle-info

If the Impression indicator is not green, [find the fix here.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-75d19063-242b-486e-b874-ed3aeb011c24)

If the Click indicator is not green, [find the fix here.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-87812b65-8d1a-4fe4-adb0-06debb085501)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FJ8AFWrXwRJRJ0t5iAp1q%2Fclick%2520check.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d36fc82&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-2.-disable-a-d-unit-during-popups-and-overlays)

2\. **Disable Ad unit During Popups and Overlays**

Ensure that when a popup or overlay appears over an ad unit, the background ad unit is disabled to prevent accidental clicks, avoiding potential policy issues due to high CTR.

circle-info

To disable the ad, call HideAd() on nativeAdHolder, and to enable it again use UnHideAd()

circle-exclamation

Ensure the ad unit is disabled even when it's completely hidden by the overlay.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FnOcWD5wvWMSl7jtjcT1D%2FAdUnit%2520Overlay.gif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7668e791&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-3.-enable-status-visualizer)

3\. **Enable Status Visualizer:**

Before sending a build to our QA for testing, ensure the Status Visualizer is enabled.

circle-info

**You don't need to disable it;** **it will be automatically hidden** when Test Mode is disabled in PubScale Settings.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FbEnZ8ngIWno9uww2VpKz%2FStatusVisualizer.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6a73f69&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-4.-a-d-request-management)

4\. **Ad Request Management:**

**To Allow Subsequent Ad Requests:**

circle-exclamation

This is to be done only if your ad is placed on **panels or pop-ups**

If your ad is placed on panels or popups, disable AutoFetch() and manually call FetchAd() only when the UI panel or overlay is active.

When fetching an ad manually, include a counter. If it has been over 15 seconds since the last ad impression, fetch a new one; otherwise, continue showing the current ad.

circle-info

Subscribing to Event\_OnAdLoaded on NativeAdHolder records the last ad load time. This prevents multiple ad requests, especially during frequent panel openings and closings.

**Avoid Ad Unit Triggering Multiple Requests:**

To address this issue, ensure that AutoFetch() is disabled whenever FetchAd() is called manually.

**5\. Rollout with A/B Test**

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FLDwImFjlmPOUlgbipNpH%2F165_benefits_AB_testing_illustration_blog.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81c68e09&sv=2)

If you plan to roll out with an A/B test where ads are shown to some of the users while others don't see them, make sure to follow the steps below:

1.  The first step would be to **remove the PubScaleManager prefab from the first scene**
    
2.  Once a response is received from the A/B test service (such as Firebase Remote config)
    
    1.  If the user is to be shown ads, you can instantiate PubScaleManager like any GameObject or it can also be loaded from the Resources folder
        
    2.  Once the PubScaleManager is instantiated, it will begin Caching Ads
        
    
3.  In addition to the above, the **default state of all Native ad Game Objects needs to be Disabled.** Otherwise, when the native ad object requests an ad, the PubScaleManager will get dynamically instantiated (lazy loaded) and begin caching ads.
    

The main goal is to prevent the PubScaleManager from being loaded for users who are not supposed to see ads. If active, it will cache ads that will not get shown, impacting Show Rate negatively driving down ecpm.

Doing the above steps (2) and (3) ensures the A/B test happens correctly.

[PreviousTesting the integrationchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/testing-the-integration)
[NextTroubleshootchevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Visual Checks:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#visual-checks)
    
*   [Functional Checks:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#functional-checks)

# NativeAdHolder | Immersive Ads SDK

Native Ad Holders communicate with the PubScaleManager to send ad requests and receive ad fills. It is the packaging unit of a single native ad placement in your scene and handles how and when to make Ad requests.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#properties)

Properties:

Name

Description

**AdResizeScale**

Allows adjusting the ad scale globally for all Fixed aspect ratio Display handlers to fit inside the available space for the ad. To use a custom value for a specific aspect ratio, it can be done in the NativeAdDisplayHandler inspector settings.

AdBadgeFrame

Assign a global Ad badge for all Fixed aspect ratio ad display handlers. Alternatively, similar AdResizeScale, a custom ad badge can be assigned in the NativeAdDisplayHandler to override the global Ad Badge.

**adTag**

This tag is used to identify an Ad placement in your game to track log events. Make sure they are unique.

**canvas**

Reference to the parent canvas component.

**placeholder**

This game object will be shown before the Ad loads and will get disabled once the ad is loaded.

**adDisplay**

Reference to the default [NativeAdDisplayHandlerarrow-up-right](https://github.com/GreedyGame/sdkone-unity_native_ads_plugin/wiki/NativeAdDisplayHandler)
 component which will determine how the native ad is shown once it is loaded.

**UseExtraFormats (**Custom Aspect Formats**)**

Boolean that tells the SDK to search the extra landscape and portrait formats at runtime when set to true. Otherwise, it will use only the default format assigned to adDisplay field.

**landscapeAdFormats**

List of NativeAdDisplayHandlers tailored for Ads with a Landscape product image.

**portraitAdFormats**

List of NativeAdDisplayHandler tailored for Ads with a Portrait product image.

**nonMediaType**

List of NativeAdDisplayHandler which handles cases when the advertisement does not have a product image.

**AD FETCH OPTIONS**

**AutoFetch**

If enabled, the Ad will automatically be requested in OnEnable for the Game Object

**TriggerFetchWithCollider**

If enabled, the Ad request will be made when a collider with a certain tag enters inside the bounds of the attached collider component. Make sure the IsTrigger is checked for the collider

**TriggerOnCollisionWithTag**

The game object Tag that will trigger the Ad request if TriggerFetchWithCollider is enabled

If both the above are deselected, the Ad Holder expects you to invoke FetchAd() manually from another script

**RefreshRate**

The Native Ad Holder makes a new ad request using this delay value after an impression is registered on the current ad displayed. The recommended value is 30s after an impression.

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#public-methods)

Public Methods:

All these methods can be overloaded

Name

Description

**FetchAd**

Generates request for a new Ad.

**HideAd**

(⚠️ Native Ads can register click events even if they are overlapped by other UI components.) The AdDisplayHandler is disabled, and the placeholder object is activated. This prevents the ad from registering an unintentional click.

**UnHideAd**

Re-show the ad once the overlapping UI is not active

**StopRefresh**

Stops the Ad unit refresh calls.

**ResetTriggerByColliderAdFetchCondition**

Resets the condition to trigger a FetchAd call when using Collider as trigger

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#events)

Events

Name

Description

**Event\_AdRequest**

The event is raised before the referenced **NativeAdHolder** component requests a new Ad from the ad cache.

**Event\_OnNativeAdActive**

This static event is raised when any **NativeAdHolder** component gets activated in the scene.

**Event\_OnAdLoaded**

The event is raised when the referenced **NativeAdHolder** component receives its Ad fill from the ad cache.

**Event\_OnAdFillNotReceivedInThisAttempt**

The event is raised when there is no ad present in the cache at the time of the request by the NativeAdHolder

**Event\_OnAdImpression**

The event is raised when the referenced **NativeAdHolder** component registers an impression for the loaded Ad.

**Event\_OnAdClicked**

The event is raised when the referenced **NativeAdHolder** component registers a click for the active Ad.

**Event\_OnAdValuePaid**

The event is raised when the impression-level revenue is available for the current impression.

*   Please make sure to subscribe to Event\_AdRequest in the Awake() callback in order not to miss the Auto-Fetch **Event\_AdRequest,** which is triggered in OnEnable()
    

[PreviousPubScaleManagerchevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Properties:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#properties)
    
*   [Public Methods:](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#public-methods)
    
*   [Events](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#events)

# Changing Ad Visuals | Immersive Ads SDK

Customizing the look of the ads is as simple as switching out image assets on specific game objects in the hierarchy and changing the text and image colors. Additionally, you may also reposition and resize some of the UI elements.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FFMiZCOwx25tzDwZ5tnBe%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25209.29.36%2520AM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d295a370&sv=2)

MediaLandscapeSimple

For this example, we consider the MediaLandscapeSimple display handler template. The steps discussed will apply to all other display templates as well.

**CHANGING IMAGE ASSETS**

The starting point of changing the look of the ad is by changing the ad background. This can be done by changing the source image of the Image component on the Display Template root object.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FVYWJ9lIjx8Cwiw8mNqZX%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25209.45.46%2520AM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1912aef8&sv=2)

Let's consider a Game with a Starry Night visual theme

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FVnmaAJi6ZudHXSrwFGQI%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25209.48.43%2520AM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=68220456&sv=2)

After changing the Ad background, we can change the source images on certain child objects to further customize the look of the ad.

OBJ NAME

CHANGE ?

COMMENTS

BigImg

No

This gets assigned at runtime by the Advertiser Large image asset

AdIconImg

No

This gets assigned at runtime by the Advertiser Icon image asset

ButtonCta

Yes

You can use the button UI asset from the game here

AdTag

Yes

You can also switch out the default ad tag with your custom AdTag asset

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FNV3FysVTyQTsnfGse7ow%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%252010.15.12%2520AM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=277af648&sv=2)

There could be other image objects in the ad display hierarchy, which serve only an aesthetic purpose and can be customized. An example of such an object would be the lower rectangle panel in the above image which groups the logo, headline, rating, and CTA button.

**CHANGING COLORS**

In addition to colors on the image component, the text colors can be changed as per the colors in your game

OBJ NAME

CHANGE?

COMMENTS

AdHeadlineTxt

Yes

Found in all Display Templates as it is a required field

AdCtaTxt

Yes

Found in all Display Templates as it is a required field

BodyTxt

Yes

Is an optional field. Not present in all Display Templates.

StarTypeTxt

Yes

Is an optional field

BigImg

No

Will be set to white at runtime to preserve the look of the Large image provided by the Advertiser

AdIconImg

No

Will be set to white at runtime to preserve the look of the Small Icon image provided by the Advertiser

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2Fr2KXijv2kDfreQ3Db5Dc%2Fg5.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76987fc5&sv=2)

\*NOTE: The Logo and Large Product Image on the right are SAMPLES for illustration purposes

* * *

And that's all there is to customize the look of an Ad Display Template.

You can go ahead and customize other Display Templates as well - MediaLandscapeBlur, MediaPotrait, and NonMedia. The same steps apply with minor variations.

Here's an example of the ad in a game with wooden visual theme:

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FcCFJaye24DLZTvUOCy6K%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25202.36.56%2520PM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3479e185&sv=2)

In addition to this, you can adjust the position of individual elements by changing values in the RectTransform and the built-in Unity UI Layout components.

* * *

CHANGING AD SIZE:

The Ad size can be changed by adjusting the Rect Transform scale.

The important pointer to keep in mind is to make sure the scaling is uniform (Same values for X and Y)

CHANGING AD SHAPE:

You can change the Ad Shape by changing the width and height value of the Rect Transform on the Root Object (SS\_NativeAd or WS\_NativeAd)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2F8ZTczcpj9Rv5Y8O52uFK%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25204.58.51%2520PM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f81af3a3&sv=2)

This will impact both MediaType as well NonMediaType display templates

If you want to change only one of these categories, then instead of the Root object you can adjust the Left, Right, Top, and Bottom padding values on the MediaType or NonMediaType objects.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FiUBaXDuujA5XfwHIXeg4%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25208.14.41%2520PM.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1cc9008&sv=2)

In this case, you could disable the Image component on the root game object (SS\_NativeAd or WS\_NativeAd) to remove the light gray background.

Once new values are set, you may need to adjust the properties on certain child elements depending on the structure of the Display template. Make sure to test adjusted values across different display resolutions

[PreviousAd Object Structurechevron-left](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/ad-object-structure)
[NextExtra Display Templateschevron-right](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates)

# Extra Display Templates | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates#using-a-single-display-template)

USING A SINGLE DISPLAY TEMPLATE

To use a single display template (for instance MediaLandscapeSimple), do the following in the NativeAdHolder component.

1.  Assign MediaLandscapeSimple to the DEFAULT DISPLAY FORMAT field
    
2.  Uncheck the ADD EXTRA DISPLAY FORMATS field
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2443726033-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%252Fuploads%252FmKe0Gq8EKvMvSkPrloln%252F1%2520ADD%2520EXTRA%2520FORMATS.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a0bab28-8b98-4d93-9e2b-1af5acf7d9f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7b9f69d&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates#additional-display-templates)

ADDITIONAL DISPLAY TEMPLATES

The Display Handler Templates used in the default Ad Prefabs are:

1.  MediaLandscapeSimple
    
2.  MediaLandscapeBlur
    
3.  MediaPotrait
    
4.  NonMedia
    

In addition to the above display templates, the SDK provides the following templates:

1.  LogoHeadlineCompact (New! added in 1.4.2)
    
2.  LongHorizontalSimple
    
3.  LongHorizontalSimple2
    
4.  LongVerticalSimple
    
5.  TemplateCombo1
    
    1.  Combo1 Landscape
        
    2.  Combo1 Portrait
        
    
6.  TemplateCombo2
    
    1.  Combo2 Landscape
        
    2.  Combo2 Portrait
        
    
7.  TemplateCombo3
    
    1.  Combo3 Landscape
        
    2.  Combo3 Portrait
        
    

These can be found in the path:

Assets/PubscaleSDK/NativeAds/Prefabs/DisplayTemplates/Dynamic/

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%2Fblobs%2FY6FGqA9ypCZYBLO0mosw%2FLogoCompact.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a42a2c0e&sv=2)

New LogoHeadlineCompact template

circle-exclamation

Make sure to assign the reference to NativeAdHolder in the CheckLogo script if using this template

TO USE THESE FORMATS:

1.  Drag and drop the Display Template as a child to the SS\_NativeAd or (WS\_NativeAd > Canvas) object
    
2.  If using a Single Template, follow the steps from the section above
    
3.  If using multiple templates
    
    1.  Make sure the ADD EXTRA DISPLAY FORMATS is checked
        
    2.  Remove any display templates that you don't want to use from the Display options array
        
    3.  Add the new display templates to the array for the SDK to pick at runtime depending on the Ad big media aspect ratio
        
    
4.  Assign the Default Display Template
    
5.  Make sure the Status Visualizer is visible!
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2443726033-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%252Fuploads%252FxbdGt596nuVSRqh9twCH%252F2%2520ADD%2520EXTRA%2520FORMATS.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db763022b-4a82-448d-91c1-8d5c96793e33&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aef3d99b&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates#custom-display-templates-create-your-own-template)

CUSTOM DISPLAY TEMPLATES (CREATE YOUR OWN TEMPLATE)

*   If you create your own Custom Display Template, create a variant for portrait big image media as well.
    
*   This will ensure the Ad unit looks good when the ad's big image media is in Portrait aspect ratio.
    
*   In this case, you have to add your custom display variants to the Display Options array as shown in the steps below
    

1.  Set **\`****ADD EXTRA DISPLAY FORMATS****\`** field to Enabled
    
2.  Remove any default display templates that you don't want to use from the Display options array
    
3.  Add your Custom display templates to the array for the SDK to pick at runtime, depending on the ad's big media aspect ratio
    
4.  Make sure the Status Visualizer is visible
    
5.  Done!
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2443726033-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fyi7AJIrqv3A12rV6WjHM%252Fuploads%252FiCpnR8ZVMNeDXFIgOIYo%252F3%2520ADD%2520EXTRA%2520FORMATS%2520v2.6.0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D952243a5-fd3e-4383-87f8-7cc7d7c73907&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f700b5a&sv=2)

Custom Display Templates
